Woaa hwee sɛ ɔdehyee no na ɛyɛ mmeamena afi sɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ hɔ biara: Wɔhwee sɛ ɛyɛ sɛ nsuo a ɛwɔ asase so no, nnyigyei a ɛwɔ asase so no, na biribiara nanso ɛnyɛ mmeamena na ɛde ne ho ayɛ mmeamena. **(A more natural/colloquial version, prioritizing flow and common phrasing, would be):** Woaa hwee sɛ ɔdehyee no yɛ sɛ wɔn a ɛwɔ hɔ biara a ɛyɛ mmeamena: Wɔhwee sɛ ɛyɛ nnyigyei, nnyigyei a ɛwɔ asase so, na biribiara nanso ɛnyɛ mmeamena a ɛde ne ho ayɛ mmeamena. **Explanation of Choices & Nuances:** * **ɔdehyee:** Sun. (Literally, "the royal one"). * **ɛyɛ mmeamena afi sɛ:** operates on the same principles as/is similar to. * **wɔn a wɔwɔ hɔ biara:** all other stars (literally, “those that are there, all”). * **Wɔhwee sɛ:** They found that/It was discovered that. * **nsuo a ɛwɔ asase so no, nnyigyei a ɛwɔ asase so no:** luminosity, rotation. I used "nsuo" (water/light) to convey luminosity and "nnyigyei" (spinning/rotation). Using direct equivalents for astronomical terms can sometimes sound unnatural in Twi. The "a ɛwɔ asase so" (which is on the earth) is added to further clarify the term. * **na biribiara nanso ɛnyɛ mmeamena:** and nothing else but. * **a ɛde ne ho ayɛ mmeamena:** that drives it/makes it function. **Important Notes:** * Twi doesn't always have direct equivalents for complex scientific terms. The translation aims for conceptual accuracy and natural-sounding language. * There are different dialects of Twi (Asante, Akuapem, etc.). This translation is geared toward Asante Twi, the most widely spoken form. * The sentence is quite complex, so achieving a perfectly elegant and concise translation while preserving all nuances is challenging. I've prioritized clarity and understandability.

Ɛyɛ adwuma a ɛyɛ dodoɔ ma ɛnne deɛ ɛwɔ UK biara, nanso mmrahyɛ ahorow a ɛwɔ Scotland yɛ denkyɛm, na abusuakyire a edi so no ahua sɛ ɛma abofra mu nni dwuma.
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛ Pamela Ferguson, na ɛwɔ Dundee University no, deɛ ɔka kyerɛ sɛ, "afa akyi no, ɛte sɛ ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛ wobɛyɛ adwuma bi na wosusu sɛ wobɔ afɔnno wɔ abofrafo a wɔne abusuafuo no ho."
Ɔsom no ho no, na ɛwɔ mfiridwuma a ɛwɔ ntaban no, aka kyerɛkyerɛfo sɛ wonnni nkɔso kyɛ akyiri, ɛwɔ fie a wɔde atwekyekyereɛ no.
Wɔahyɛ sɛ, abakɔsɛm no, sɛnea ɛbɔɔ baa, deɛ bɛkyerɛ wɔ mu no, ɛbɛma mmeae a Palestine di kan de abɛyɛ hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ akyiri 1967 mfinfini no.
Maddi akyerɛ deɛ, osrammafoɔ no ne Yerusalem sɛ́deɛ bɛbɔn fii ase, ɛyɛ sɛnkyireɛ mmienu a yɛahyehyɛ ma no, ne Jordan Valley nimdeɛ no nso.
Israɛl na ɛde bɛyɛ sɛ, sɛ ɛsɛn kyerɛw a, ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɛwɔ asɛn a ɛwɔ abɔnten so dodoɔɔ mfe dumɛnsa, na Palestine Authority nso de bɛyɛ sɛ na ɛbɛsɔre akyi mfe dumɛnan.
Abusuapanyin a yɛde yɛn abɔdeɛ no mu nhyehyɛe no nyae sɛ wɔde abɔdeɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛyɛ den no hwɛ so, ɛfie ne ɛhwehwɛ nanso ɛso nka a ɛyɛ ahyia no.
Mmarima a ɛyɛ mmeabusɛm a wɔde wɔn ahyɛ mu, na ɛwɔ National Parks and Wildlife Service (NPWS) ne Sporting Shooters Association of Australia (NSW) Inc. no mu, wɔfaa wɔn fii ase, wɔn a wɔyɛ abɔde ahorow a ɛwɔ Sporting Shooters Association de nnwom kwan no so.
Abofra Mick O'Flynn, ɔkyerɛwfo a ɛwɔ National Parks and Wildlife Service (NPWS) mu, a na ɔyɛ Park Conservation and Heritage Director no, deɛ ɛbɛyɛ mfeɛsɛm a ɛto so abien no, na wɔde ama nnwoma a ɛyɛ den a ɛkyerɛ sɛnea wobɛyɛ kwan so na wɔhwehwɛɛ wɔn.
Martelly yɛɛ asempa akyi sɛ yɛbɛyɛ abusuapanyin a wɔde nnwomaso kyere mu no (CEP) a ɛwɔ mmiɛnsa a ɛyɛ den kyerɛw no awiaafo anadwo.
Ɛyɛ Martelly no mu nnan anan de akyiri mfe anan.
Ɛyɛ mfeɛ akyi no, aban no abusuapanyin a ɛwɔ hɔ no de nkyerekyereɛ sɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛyɛ denkyem no tumi nsa no de, na wɔde akyɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔgye n'adwuma fi so sɛ ebia ɛbɛyɛ adwuma no biara a ɛbɛyɛ yɛn so, na ɛbɛyɛ abusuapanyin no nya yɛn so. **(Alternatively, a slightly more concise and commonly used phrasing):** Ɔda wɔn akyi mfeɛ akyi no, ɔman no abusuapanyin a ɛwɔ hɔ no kyee sɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛ a edi kan no tumi nsa no de, na wɔde akyɛ sɛ ɔsɛ sɛ ɔgye n'adwuma fi so, na ebi nso wɔde ahyɛ mfeɛ a ɛbɛba no so.**
Komisno no na ɛyɛ Martelly abusuafuo a ɛfaa so a ɛmaa akyire pɛnsoɔ a ɛbɛyɛ October na ɛsii no.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛbɛhyia a, nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛtaa hyɛ maaha no no noho kwan so sɛnea wonnɛɛ sɛ wɔnhyɛ abatoɔ a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ no afi 2011.
Ɛyɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mmerɛw a, iPod a ɛyɛ nte sɛn no abien no mu nnan na ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛtɔ so nson, na ɛde abien nson a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛtɔ so nson pɛ, na ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛtɔ so nson a, na abɔfo nson a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛtɔ so nson no.
Japan manfoɔ no Hoɔman a ɛwɔ Nnwomto ne Nnwoma ho (METI) tee sɛ wɔdwo no, wɔn a wɔdwoɔ no no, wɔdwoɔ mfeɛmpem nan anan awɔtwa a ɛfa nna horow a ɛwɔ hɔ no ho.
Ͻbɛyɛ akyiri pɔnkɔ, METI wiee sɛ Apple ayɛɛ no nhoma no mu sɛ ɛwom sɛnkyɛnnum mmiɛnsa nnan a ɛyɛ mmerɛw.
Ɔsono no tee sɛnkyɛnmaa no hyɛɛ Apple abɔdeɛ no ne nhoma abusuabo no akyi “ɛyɛ mmerɛw” sɛ nea ɛyɛ nwonwa.

Ɔkyerɛw sɛ obeafo a wɔde abrantɛ a wɔwo ho dwuma no, na ɔkyɛɛ ase wɔ Auckland National Women's Hospital no afe ha nkron ne nan (1959) mu.
Berebiara na ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ agyei mu no, Liggins fii ase kyinkyim te sɛ akyire yɛden kwan ma abrantɛ a wɔwoo no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ no wɔ ne ntamfo ho no.

Xinhua atwerɛn no nyɛnkyɛn sɛ abanfoɔ deɛ na ɛyɛ mmoa a wɔhyɛn wɔn nkyɛn a, wo Wukuropɔn no nea ɛwɔ hɔ biara a ɛkyerɛ mmoa a wɔde awo mmoa a ɛkyerɛ wo ha no, wɔde sii nnaa.
Ɛna afãfo a wɔyɛ abɛsɛ no nso baa yɛ Luna ase.
Tommy Dreamer na ɛyɛ sɛ, “Luna na ɛyɛ mmaa a edi kan sɛ Extreme Ɔhemmaa. Ɔyɛ me yɛni biako a ɔdanee nni dwuma no. Luna wuu no da a ɔbɔɔ mu mmeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ. Ɛyɛ adwuma biara nanso ɛyɛ sɛ ɔno. Ɔbarima a ɛte sɛ ɔbarima.”
Dustin "Goldust" Runnels kae sɛ, "Luna yɛ sɛ me – anaa wo ho yɛ me sɛn pii deɛ, ɛyɛ sɛ ɔyɛ me sɛn pii biara…mepɛ wo dodo, na mebɛhyia wo…mebɛhyia sɛ w’ani nnye me mma mu."

Ɛna abɔde ahorow a wɔhyɛ nneɛma ho asɛm no mu no, ɔha biara nnan (29%) nim sɛ Australia bɛyɛ abusuapanyin a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛso, nanso ɔha biara nnan (31%) nso nim sɛ Australia nnyɛ abusuapanyin biara.

Ɛnyɛ mmoa a ɛyɛ mfiase a ɛde baa, na nkuo a ɛwɔ asase so no nso nni kum Wembley, na ɛnyɛ yɛbɛboa mmoa a ɛwɔ nnwom so na nso ɛnyɛ yɛbɛboa nnwom a ɛyɛ mfiase a ɛwɔ abɔso no.
Mmoa a wonnim sɛ yɛbɛn nnyigyi akyi ne nnyigyi no nso sɛ ɛbɛyɛ sɛ yɛbɛma nnyigyi no nhyehyɛeɛ biara nkyɛn nni hɔ a ɛwɔ abɔdeɛ no a wɔn a wɔda so no.
Akyinhyee a ɛfaa iraa daadaa wɔ abofra Science ase mantam no, akyiri mu yɛsɔre kyɛ sɛ nkyene a ɛtwaa nso a ɛyɛ nwoa wɔ Ekuadɔ Galápagos nanhyɛn no mu.
Ahyeagyafoɔ a ɛwɔ Princeton University, Amerika Nnwɔtwe ne Uppsala University, Sweden, ayɛ sɛ nnedua foforo no deɛ, na ɛbɔɔ wo mfeɛ pii sɛnea wogye di no, woyi mu nnan akyi na wosii anaa, efisɛ Geospiza fortes, a ɛyɛ abɔdeɛ nnedua a ɛwɔ hɔ no, ne Geospiza conirostris, a ɛnso yɛ nnedua a wɔbɔɔ abɔdeɛ ho, nnan akyi a wɔde bɛhyiaa.
Aha yɛte sɛnea wɔbɛtumi de abɔdeɛ ahenni biara ayɛ, na ɛma yɛahu sɛ yɛbɛtumi ayɛ nsoɔm a ɛyɛ kɛseɛ no sɛ mmea a ɛyɛ te sɛ nsu.
Ɛkyere sɛ ɛte sɛe sɛ wobenya mu na ɛyɛ mmea a ɛte sɛ agoro, na ɛkyɛ akyerɛ na ɛyɛ abowdwee. Ɛkyɛ akyerɛ sɛ ɛte sɛe sɛ wobɛtumi akwada mu a wobɛhyɛ mmea biara a ɛyɛ nsua, na ɛkyɛ akyerɛ na wobɛtwa mu a wobɛbɔ abowdwee. **However, a more natural and concise translation would be:** Ɛkyere sɛ wobɛtena mu na ɛyɛ mmea a ɛte sɛ agoro a ɛkyɛ akyerɛ na ɛyɛ abowdwee. Ɛkyɛ akyerɛ sɛ wobɛakwada mu a wobɛhyɛ mmea a ɛyɛ nsua, na wobɛtwa mu a wobɛbɔ abowdwee. **Explanation of choices and nuances:** * **"Ɛkyere sɛ"** - "It means/It shows that" - a common way to introduce a description. * **"wobɛtena mu"** - "it can be drawn/pulled" - more natural than literally translating "pulled into". * **"mmea a ɛte sɛ agoro"** - "thin like wire". Directly translates "thin wire." * **"ɛkyɛ akyerɛ na ɛyɛ abowdwee"** - "it can be twisted and plaited" * **"wobɛakwada mu"** - "it can be hammered" * **"mmea a ɛyɛ nsua"** - "sheets" (literally "thin things") * **"wobɛtwa mu a wobɛbɔ abowdwee"** - "it can be rolled and made into braids" (or plaited)
Ɛkyɛ sɛ wotumi ayɛ no hwɛɛ na woatumi ama no aba yɛmma afiri biara. Ɛkyɛ sɛ wotumi ayɛ no hwɛɛ bio sɛ na ɛyɛe sɛ wɔtaa de yɛɛ nkitahosow a ɛwɔ mmaa a wɔatwerɛdeɛ no mu, na ɛyɛ "illuminated manuscripts" a wɔfrɛ no.
Ɛyɛ sɛ yɛfrɛ no kemikal no pH. Ɛba sɛ wo te sɛ wosusu ho kwan ma wo a, wo pɛ sɛ wo de abɛduru a ɛyɛ kyɛw no no mu akyɛw bi.
Nsuo a ɛyɛ sɛ cabbage no yɛ sɛn pɛnkyɛnno no, ɛyɛ din sɛ ɛyɛ acid kɛseɛ, anaa ɛyɛ alkaline kɛseɛ.
pH no no mu yɛ denkyɛm a ɛwɔ abɔdeɛ no mu no na ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔdɔm a ɛwɔ abɔdeɛ a yɛsɔ no mu no te sɛn.
Hydrogen ions yɛ proton a yɛsiane wɔn mfeanom akyiri sɛ hydrogen atom no bi proton biara na elektron biara.
Kaakyire awoowɔn deɛ ɛyɛ den no abɔ wo soro na ɛka bom, afei nsa aduro a ɛhyew a woanya nkyɛn na ama woato no mu kɔkɔ.
Nsuo a ɛwɔ nsa mu no reba ma apuei no, na ɛbɛma wo nsa te sɛ dɔn a, na ɛyɛ mmera bi.
Ɛsɛm a ɛwɔ Harappa ne Mohenjo-daro manman akyi no, wɔn adɔm a ɛyɛ dɛ a ɛwɔ nyinaa mu no, na ɛwɔ mpesa a ɛyɛ den kyerɛw bi a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wim biara a ɛyɛ baabi te sɛ mpesa no.
Minoan Mantam a ɛwɔ Greece man mu, Crete ne Santorini nam, mu no, abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu kyekyɛ sɛ wosɛe abɔneɛ a ɛyɛɛ sɛnkyi a ɛyɛ mmerɛw afiri.
Na ɛwɔ nsua a ɛyɛ dɔm wɔ Misraim, Persia ne Chinaa nyinaa akyiri sɛnea ɛte bi. Na wɔ Roma man mu no, nsua a ɛyɛ dɔm som sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ nkitahodie a mma mmea ne mmɛni yɛba ha wɔ tebea biara mu.
Ɛwom sɛ wotua obi a ɛyɛ mmyɛnsa afã horow a, na wobɛyɛ sɛ wode satɛliti yɛ.
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ no bɛyɛ sɛnea wotumi ahyehyɛ no na akyiri no nso yɛkyerɛ no abubu so, bio nso yɛsan abubu no abɛyɛ sɛ yɛteɛ wɔ hɔ bio.
Ɛyɛ sɛ onipa a wɔde kyɛrekyɛre a ɛwɔ hɔ no na ɛyɛɛ sɛ wobɛyɛ nnyigyei kɔ soro. Abɔdeɛfo de mmea a ɛwɔ soro mu yɛ nhoma, ɛfie koraa nso, nti ɛyɛ sɛ asase no abɔnten no bɛtumi ayɛ mmaa a yɛde hu no nyinaa nhyehyɛe.
Ɛyɛ bɛyɛ rakɛt a ɛyɛ pɛpɛpɛpɛ sɛnkyɛ mu nnan no, na ɛtrɛw sɛnkyɛ mu anaa adwuma bi a ɛkyerɛ nyansahyɛfoɔ a ɛyɛ ɔpɛpɔn no.
Kyɛre no abɛyɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mmerɛw so na ɛde kwan ma adwuma a ɛyɛ yɛn ho mfeɛ. Nnwonkora a kyɛre no abɛyɛ sɛ ɛyɛ yɛn ho mfeɛ ne sɛ ɛde yɛn kwan sii fa bi, na yɛhu kwan sɛ yɛbɛyɛ mfeɛ.
Ɛde hyɛn no, ɛde kɔkɔdɔ, na ɛde nneɛma pii a yɛde ahyia.
Asew no ho yɛɛɛ, wɔn anim a ɛyɛ mfeɛ nanso ɛnyɛ dwo, na ɛma mfeɛ nanso ɛnyɛ dwo a ɛyɛ nuna a ɛda nnuru, dwumakɔ, ne asasepanin.
Aanaa na, wɔnkyɛ sɛ wɛwɛɛ nsuo a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a, nanso ɛsono nsuo a ɛyɛ pii no na ɛde nsuo a ɛyɛ mmerɛw no a, te sɛ abɔdeɛ, apim, adwoa, na mmoa. **(Alternative, slightly more colloquial and potentially clearer depending on context):** Bio nso, wɔwɔ nkyɛnkyɛn panyin a wɔde abɔdeɛ, apim, adwoa, ne mmoa te sɛɛ a yɛmma no. Wɔn mu nso yɛwɔ abɔdeɛ a wɔatumi mfa sɛ wɔnkyɛ a.
Sorekyɛm a wɔdwi so no ne mmeamuna a onnim a wonnim nea wonnim no, wɔn a wɔwɔ nnyigyi kwan a ɔne ne ho hyia a ɛyɛn na ɛma wɔn nhyɛ nnaano anaa nea ɛka ho.
Mpembaɔw no ne abɔfra a wɔdwo no kɛseɛ, na wɔte sɛ́ wɔwɔ apapansin a wɔfrɛ no "pride".
Mmea a ɛwɔ hɔ no bi nkyekyɛm a ɛwɔ mmarima pii a wɔwɔ mfaahɔ so, a ɛwɔ mmarima abubuo kosi mmarima mmienu a wɔn ho yɛ den, te sɛ abofra a ɛwɔ akyiri pii a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mmea mmienu a ɛyɛ mmienu, a ɛwɔ abofra a ɛyɛ mmienu.
Abofrafoɔ no biara a ɛsono wɔn ho, na ɛyɛ abusua pii a ɛwɔ abofra ne mma.
Abrafo a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ sɛ wɔn mu yɛ pɛ sɛ wolofɔ ne asaase mmoa, mmoa a ɛyɛ nwonwa biara sɛ abrafo (nanso ɛnyɛ nkyɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛte ase) wɔ mmɔfra mu, a na ɛyɛ mfeafɔ sɛ wɔn a wɔpɔn no.
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛ a yɛhu kwan so, ɔhene a ɛtwaa nso bɛkɔ so (nanso ɛnyɛ yɛyɛ), bɛtumi nso nya, bɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ nanso bɛtumi ayɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ sɛ onipa bɔtabɔ ne nsa mu pɛn no mu nnan.
Ɔkyena a ɛwɔ mfinfin no, ɛwɔ mmea ananmu a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn (Genus Panthera) biako pɛ na ɛsono, ɛnyɛm, na ɛbɔbea. Ɛsono a ɛnnum a ɛte sɛɛ no na ɛwɔ mmea a anaa nkanea a ɛnya nkasa.
Ɔkyena no sɛ́e no nnyigye sɛ ɔhene no sɛ́e kɛseɛ, ɛnyɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mmeɛa a ɛsɛe nnam, na ɛyɛ sɛ abɔdeɛ a ɛte sɛ obi a ɔgyaakoa, na ɔbɔɔ no.
Akyekyew a, w’apere sɛ ocelot no na ɛbɛyɛ mmea a ɛyɛ te sɛn a ɛde hyɛ. Ɛno akyiri abofra, nnaa, kofiriw a ɛyɛ mmea ne nkyɛn a ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ adeakyee a ɛyɛ mmea. Ɔcelot no a ɛyɛ adwumayɛfo no, mmea biara a ɛde hyɛ no yɛ te sɛn a ɛyɛ kɛse a ɛyɛ nnoɔ no.
Abɔdeɛfo no bɛyɛ sɛ ocelots de nte sɛnso akyerɛkyerɛ nneɛma a wɔde hyɛ nsa mu na woakye wɔn a wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔnya (nhwɛfo) wɔ asase so.
Wɔte sɛ wɔboa afiri mu yɛ denkyem, na wɔnya ntam no nso yɛ den. Abrafo akyee wɔn nhwɛfoɔ de wɔn ho hyia nnanwɔtwe, afei wɔbɔ wɔn so.
Berebi a obi a yɛn nnoɔ bi (mmea a ɛyɛ bɛyɛ pii) kɔ so nkyereɛ nnoɔ kɛseɛ a na ɛwɔ hɔ no (te sɛ sɛ wɔkɔ so kɔ apem panyin no akyiri, yare no akyiri, anaa sɛ wɔkɔ island foforo nanso wonni mfa so kɔ wo hɔ akyiri), wobɛhunu denam ntetee foforoɛ bi a na ɛwɔ hɔ no.
Ɛda kwan so no, ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ nneɛma pii ne asɛmpresa pii nso, enti mmea no a w’afee no bɛhwehwɛ nneɛma foforo a ɛbɛyɛ mmerɛw anaa nneɛma a ɛbɛboa wɔn sɛ wɔbɛyɛ asɛmpresa te sɛ ɛbɛyɛe no saa ara a ɛdii wɔn din no.
Mfe a edi kan no nni mu yɛn ara, na wonhwɛ nneɛma pɛn pɛn a wodi kan no bio.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea bere biara bɛyɛ, sɛ nna anaa ahokɔ ahorow bɛte sɛe nna ha biara a wɔde bɛto saa abrabɔ yi mu no, wɔn nsaeɛ ahorow no de bɛyɛ nna afoforo no nsaeɛ ahorow a ɛnni no de.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛ, wɔn a wɔyɛ mfe numnum pii sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ mfe a ɛyɛ pii de, aane a wɔn a wɔte sɛnea wɔte no, ɛno a ɛyɛ den no nso bebua mu.
Yɛfrɛ sɛ́deɛ no speciation, na ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mmaa foforɔ bi a ɛyɛ mmaa a ɛhwehwɛ. Speciation yɛ mfasoɔ a ɛnte sɛe a ɛwɔ mmaa mmaa nhyehyɛeɛ mu, na ɛyɛ paara biara.
Mmea a ɛyɛ oxygen a yɛn homa, na yɛde carbon-dioxide a yɛn huu a yɛhwehwɛ no.
Abotan no de hyɛn na ɛyɛ nnam wɔ nhyehyɛeɛ mu. Na ɛma nea ɛtwe abotam de nso.
Yɛtaa yɛ nsua nyinaa fi ntaa dekyɛn na yɛtaa yɛ ahwɛfoɔ fi ntaa. Ɛbɛɛ sɛ ɛsɛn a yɛdii yɛ no nyinaa yɛ ntaa. Ntaa nni hɔ a, nwanini a ɛbɛn akyiri a ɛnnaa nnwe.
Mosasaurus na ɛyɛɛ wɔn akwan so sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ bi, enti na ɛnni hwee biara, efisɛ mosasaurus foforo no.
Mempɔn yawkyɛ a ɛyɛ denkyɛm, a ɛwɔ mpaninfoɔ no mu nsono, ɛyɛ sɛ mpaninfoɔ no mu biara a ɛkyere no, ɛnnye yɛn a ɛkyere no. **(Note:** This is a complex sentence and achieving a *perfect* stylistic equivalent in Twi is difficult without more context. This translation prioritizes accuracy of meaning. There are several ways to phrase parts of it, and a native speaker might choose slightly different wording for a more natural flow depending on the specific dialect and audience.)** Here's a breakdown of some key choices: * **"Its long jaws"**: "Mempɔn yawkyɛ a ɛyɛ denkyɛm" - "Its jaw that is long." ("Mempɔn" = its, "yawkyɛ" = jaw, "a ɛyɛ denkyɛm" = that is long). * **"studded with more than 70 razor-sharp teeth"**: "a ɛwɔ mpaninfoɔ no mu nsono" - "that has more than 70 teeth in its mouth." ("mpaninfoɔ no mu" = in its mouth, "nsono" = many/more than). The "razor-sharp" aspect is implied by the context of a predator. * **"along with an extra set in the roof of its mouth"**: "ɛyɛ sɛ mpaninfoɔ no mu biara a ɛkyere no" - "it is as if there are teeth also in the roof of its mouth." This is a bit more descriptive due to the concept of a 'roof of the mouth' needing explanation. * **"meaning that there was no escape for anything that crossed its path"**: "ɛnnye yɛn a ɛkyere no" - "no one can escape when it encounters it." ("ɛnnye yɛn" = no one can escape, "a ɛkyere no" = when it encounters it/when it faces it).

Ɛnaa abofrafo no ne nyinaa yɛ kwan no mu na ɛyɛ kwan a ɛde sɛ wo de abotare bɛkyerɛ agya. Dɔm a ɛyɛ dɔm no na ɛwɔ nkurow a ɛde sɛ wo de abotare bɛkyerɛ agya. Wɔde dwato a wɔde yɛ dwumɛ na wɔyɛ nkyɛn.
Na ɛnkyɛn sɛ́ Canaan asase so no, ɛnɔ́ nansa a, ɛma nnyɛn a ɛyɛ den.
Greenland no yɛɛ dɔɔso a ɛyɛ bɛyɛ. Na wɔka kyerɛ sɛ, Erik the Red bɛyɛɛ Iceland na wɔkyɛɛ no afi ma enti, sɛ ɔbɛyɛ mfiridwuma de bɛyɛ fam, ɔhwee Greenland na ɔmaa no Greenland.
Nanso ɛberɛ biara sɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ no, Eskimofoɔ adwiniw a ɛwɔ hɔ no na ɛwɔ hɔ bere a ɛyɛ.
Ɛwom sɛ ɛyɛ 'Scandinavian' man a ɛyɛ den, nanso wɔn ahenfo, abrabɔ, adwuma ne ahayifo a ɛwɔ Denmark, Sweden, Norway ne Iceland no nyinaa yɛ pɛpɛpɛ.
Ɛna woaahwehwɛɛ film no National Treasure a, ɛsɛ sɛ wo hu sɛ abofra a edi kan no abusuabɔ no akyi no ne treasure map a ɛyɛe den.
Nanso ɛnyɛ mmoa. Ɛwom sɛ ɛyɛ den kyerɛw no akyiri, nanso ɛnyɛ mmea map.
Akyiri no, wɔkyerɛɛ Declaration of Independence nnyapɔ soɔ "Original Declaration of Independence dated 4th July 1776" yi. Nsɛm no hyɛ sɛn a, w’ani gye ho na w’apue a, ɛwɔ abotɔn a ɛto so.
Ɛnyɛ yɛanyɛ sɛ ɛyɛ sɛn na ɛyɛe no, nanso ɛte sɛ asɛmpaka no a ɛyɛ dodoɔ no (ɛyɛ mita 75.575 centimeters fa 62.23 centimeters) na ɛyɛe sɛ yɛsrasrasaa no maa ɔsram.
Yɛde, ɛyɛ sɛ ɛte sɛ nea wonyaa no de sɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ kɛseɛ no.
D-Day anɔden ne ɛsɛm a ɛdi no nyinaa de France atifi no ahyiaa, na ɛdeɛ south no ara na ɛnya hɔ.
Ɛhyɛyɛɛ "Vichy" agyafo no no. Na ɛyɛ Franfo a edi mũ na edi hɔ na wɔbɔɔ wɔn ho sɛ Germanfo no wɔ afe 1940 mu, na ɛwɔn akyiri wɔn sɛ wɔbɛkwan so hwehwɛ Germanfo no nanso ɛmfa wɔn asiane hwehwɛ wɔn.
Ɔdaada hyehyɛɛ 15 Ɔbɔbue 1940, Aferɛhyia no hyɛɛ Frɛnkuro manfoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ no, nea hyɛɛ yɛn no deɛ yɛfrɛ no "Operation Dragoon".
Meda aseɛ, wobɛyɛ me sɛnea mebɛhyia wo. Ɔsono biara nna, Amerikafo ne Free French abusuakuo no de bɛyɛɛ Franse manfo no anim na na ɛsɔrekyerɛ Germany afa.
Mmrahyɛbɛ a ɛyɛ den no yɛ mmea na nnompe a nnipa pii te sɛ mmaa no fi ase, na ɛwom sɛ wɔte so dua wɔ nnompe mu, na ɛyɛ mmɔden.
Ɛdeɛ sɛ, mfeɛsɛm 'civilization' no boa wɔn sɛ ɛyɛ Latin kasa 'civilis' a ɛkyerɛ 'mmɔden', na ɛwɔ hɔ no nso na ɛkyerɛ Latin kasa 'civis' a ɛkyerɛ 'ɔmanani', na ɛkyerɛ 'ɔman so' anaa 'ɔman bi a ɛwɔ so', na ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ sɛnea ɔman no te sɛ.
Mankuma a ɛyɛ denkyemkye no ne mmara a ɛde nations bɛyɛ mfiase. Ɛkwan a ɛyɛ mmerante so yɛ anigye no kyerɛ sɛ wotumi akyerɛw sɛdeɛ wɔde abrabɔ ne ho nhoma titiriw a ɛyɛ mmerante hwehwɛ, ne akyidifoɔ nhyehyɛe a ɛte sɛ nea ɛwɔ hɔ daa, na ɛyɛ mfaso sɛ wotumi akyerɛw sɛdeɛ wohwehwɛ no.
Mmea a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛso te sɛn, bio bio no nkyinkyim a ɛde ama asɛmpka ahorow te sɛɛ a wɔde yɛ adwuma a ɛyɛ mfeɛ pii no na ɛne di nni, na emfa wɔn ho asɛm sɛ ɛyɛ mmea a ɛyɛ den.
Bere a Abrafo Ahorow ahorow no, nnaa mmarima tretre no hyɛ mmerante kwan so na ɛyɛ mmerante a, na Congress na ɛwɔ hɔ bio.
Aban no nni dwan a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛbɛtumi ayɛ mpono, na ɛfie koraa, ɛnne sɛ mmarima ne abotire a ɛkoraa no ara nni hɔ nti ɛtaa yɛn nyinaa kɔso dwuma wɔ mpaninfo a ɛwɔ manman mu, a na wɔde bɛyɛ dema ama yɛnyɛ.
Na ɛnso na ɛnkyɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɛte sɛe mmara a ɛfa mpesa ne nkitahwɛn a ɛdade wɔ manman akyi.
Nnwoma no dehyɛ sɛ mmarima nyinaa mpo akyɛ mu ayɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ biara na ɛbɛyɛ mmebusa, na mmarima de asrakyi a ɛwɔ hɔ tumfo wɔn nsa so, nti wimhyɛn a ɛwɔ asrakyi hɔ no yɛ anaa.
Italy a ɛkɔɔso dwuma a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn, ne Germany a ɛkɔɔso dwuma a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn no, ɛyɛ abrabɔ a ɛtɔ so mmiɛnsa a ɛyɛ den wɔ wiase nyinaa so, na yɛtee FIFA Dwumadi Nyinaa Abrafo a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn wɔ afeha 2006 mu.
Agodie a ɛyɛ den no mu biara ne apɔn, basketball, volleyball, mprempren, abɔkyere, nkyinkyim, tweneboa, kyekyee, abonten, nkontonkye abonten ne F1 kwan so yare.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛ, abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ hyew a ɛyɛ pɔpil wɔ faman so, akwantufo a wɔyɛ Italiyani no nso na ɛwɔ hɔ pɛpɛpɛpɛ wɔ wiase nyinaa a ɛyɛ mmoa ne Kwasida a ɛyɛ ɔmanfo nyinaa mu.
Japan ne mmeaeɛ a ɛyɛ mmienu ne nnwɔtwe senkyɛ (Honshu ne nnwɔtwe pii), na ɛma Japan bɛyɛ man a ɛto so asonnan a ɛyɛ dɔnko wɔ asase so!
Ɛfie no nuanom a Japan na ɛwɔ hɔ no nti, mpo sɛ yɛte sɛ n’abrabɔbea a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ "archipelago" no.
Taiwan fii asei kakraba wɔ afeha 15 no mu, bere a Europa mmea a wɔredi so no fii nkitahohiaa ne din sɛ Ilha Formosa, anaa aseda kɔɔso.
Mfeɛ mpem ahankron ne duowɔtwe (1624) mu no, Dɔchɛ Anaafo India Kompanie yɛɛ dwan ma wɔ Taiwan atɔe fam, na na ɛde yɛn a wɔwɔ hɔ no nyinaa yɛɛ mmea ahorɔw so a wɔtaa yɛ wɔ agodie mu na ɛyɛ mmea a wɔyɛ ade sɛ wɔboa wɔ nnwunu ne kokoo nwɛsɛn a ɛwɔ hɔ no.
Ɔda a ɛto so 1683 mu no, Qing dinasty abusuakuo (1644-1912) de Taiwan abɔdeɛ mantam no mu, mpo sɛnee ne apueɛ no nyinaa, a na ɛde Taiwan fii sɛ Qing dinasty man a ɛto so 1885 mu.
1895 mu no, Adanse-Japan Sukuupɔn a edi kan (1894-1895) mu no nyinaa mu yii no, Qing aban no bɔɔ Shimonoseki Amansɛm no, efisɛ woafori Taiwan de nyinaa maa Japan, na Japan nso hyɛn Taiwan akyi sɛ yɛbɛhyɛn 1945.
Machu Picchu no mu dɔn nsamman trɛ, ɛna ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛne Intihuatana, Ɔsunso Dwumase, ne Mmerɛw Mmiɛnsa no a ɛwɔ hɔ.
Aane wɔn a ɛwɔ mfinimfini no nyinaa ayɛ mmaa no deɛ ɛbɛyɛ sɛnea wɔdwo no kwan so, na ɛwɔ hɔ akyiri sɛ wotumi hu sɛnea ɛyɛe no bɛyɛ den no.
Abofra a ɛtɔ so nson, 1976 mu no, Machu Picchu no mu ɔha mu aduowɔn a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ aduanan no, na ɛyɛ asiane, na asiane no de bɛyɛ den kɔsii sɛnea ɛte biara.
Mme, nea ɛyɛ den koraa no, foton a ɛyɛ mmerɛw so wɔ wiase nyinaa ne 35mm, na na ɛyɛ film no sɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛpɛ wɔ analog film ntam no mu.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛte sɛnea yɛyɛ no nyinaa, nanso ɛnyɛ mmerɛw koraa, nanso ne mfaso dwumadi a ɛwɔ digiti camera ahorow no nea yɛde bɛhyɛn no ara a ɛyɛ mmerɛw.
35mm nobedwa no, wubɛyɛ sɛ ɛyɛ 36mm kɛseɛ no, na 24mm yɛ den.
Ɛdeɛ biara, saa format no nhwɛso nhyehyɛe (tweɛ mma du nhyira a ɛma wo nya mfeannwom a ɛyɛ mmoa kɛseɛ) yɛ 3:2, enti yɛka seɛ yɛyɛ no. **(Alternatively, a more concise and common phrasing):** Nanso, saa format no nhwɛso yɛ 3:2 (tweɛ mma du nhyira a ɛma wo nya mfeannwom a ɛyɛ mmoa kɛseɛ). **Explanation of choices and linguistic notes:** * **Ɛdeɛ biara:** "Therefore" or "In all respects." Used to start the sentence and establish a logical consequence. * **saa format no:** "This format." "saa" (this/that) + "format no" (the format). * **nhwɛso nhyehyɛe:** "aspect ratio". Literally "ratio arrangement" or "ratio structure." * **tweɛ mma du nhyira a ɛma wo nya mfeannwom a ɛyɛ mmoa kɛseɛ:** This is the crucial and lengthy part translating "dividing by twelve to obtain the simplest whole-number ratio." It's broken down as follows: * **tweɛ mma:** "dividing by" * **du nhyira:** "twelve" * **a ɛma wo nya:** "that makes you get/obtain" (relative clause marker) * **mfeannwom:** "numbers" * **a ɛyɛ mmoa kɛseɛ:** "that are whole/integer" (literally "are big/complete") * **yɛ 3:2:** "is 3:2". Twi generally directly incorporates numbers in this way. * **enti yɛka seɛ yɛyɛ no:** "and so we say it is so" - a common way to express "is said to be." (The second, shorter translation omits this concluding phrase for conciseness). * **Nanso:** Another alternative to Ɛdeɛ biara for "therefore". It's a more direct translation of "and so" or "but." The longer version is very precise, but may sound a little formal in everyday speech. The shorter version gets the core meaning across more naturally. I've provided both options. A native Twi speaker might slightly rephrase it depending on the context, but both are grammatically correct and understandable.
Mepɔn a ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛnea, ɛwɔ format a ɛyɛ dodoɔ no (format a ɛwɔ APS fam no, dodoɔ a) a ɛyɛ pɛpɛpɛpɛ sɛnea ɛyɛ saa aspect ratio yi ara, anaa nso ɛyɛ nnamɔfoɔ.

Ɛkyerɛ sɛ wampɛn pii no ho mmoa firi so a ɛwɔ mprempren no mu, na ɛwɔ nnan mu nkyerɛkyɛre a ɛyɛ mmerɛw no nnan so (hwɛ nhwɛso).
Bere biako mfeɛ a Europa nhyiaa mu no, Katolik Kɔmfo a ɛdɔɔso koraa ne ɛyɛ den koraa no, mmɔfra no de sii yɛn ho no.
Ɔpepem Pɔno no de abɛtɔ so adɔɔsoɔ mfe 1,000 akyi no, ɛne nea eyɛ mmeae a ɛwɔ Europa manno a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛte bi ara yɛde bɛhyia mu, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ bi nso yɛyɛ nnam.
W’asafo a ɛyɛ den no yɛɛ ntam no, na ɛde mma dɛnkyɛm pɛsɛ na ɔmanfo nyinaa.
Ɔkwan so no mu biara a ɛyɛ dɛn kɛseɛ wɔ Kristoni nyansahyɛse mu no, ɛyɛ sɛ nwanntenten a wɔde ama wɔn a wuhu nteɛ ne anidiefoɔ no, na abusuabɔ bosompra nwanntenten no wɔ hɔ bere nyia sɛ yɛhwehwɛ wɔn a wuhu nteɛ ne anidiefoɔ a ɔhyia.
Ɔsomfo no abusuakuw a ɛwɔ Roma no ara nsi hɔ anaa pa ara a ɛyɛ mfe dumogya ne afei, na saa mfaso a ɛwɔ dwadifo ne nwanwa no yɛɛ nnamfoɔ no nyinaa nkyerɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ awofereɛ biara benyaa nnamfoɔ no yɛnkyɛ.
Adomnaw no, abusuabɔ ahorow a ɛbɛyɛ sɛn no nyinaa, Britania yɛɛ dwadwenini a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛde German no hyia.
Nnwuma no yɛɛ sɛ yɛyɛe, na ɛmaa ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɛhyɛn mmoa a ɛyɛ den amannyɔ mu ne abrabɔ mu, nanso ɛnyɛ yɛn nnye abusuabɔ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ hɔ nnamɔn de koraa a ɛyɛ sɛ yɛnnye.
Britania kɔ̃ɔ no wɔ wiase nyinaa mu na ɛhyɛn mmaa biara sɛ ɛnkeka abien mu, na ɛyɛ asiane deɛ ɛyɛ mmeaa a ɛwɔ hɔ no.
Berebi sɛ yɛnso biara nni sɛnea wɔtaa yɛn ho dwuma no, Germany nso nnaasɛ sɛnea adwumangyeɛ a wɔde ahomahɔ a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ adwuma no bɛyɛ.
Ɛda 1920hyia mu no, amanɔne ne manhyia ahorow biara so sɛnea ɛyɛ bedi wɔ pacifism ne abusuabusu mu.
Akyiri sɛ wɔde ahyehyɛdeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw na ɛyɛ hyew a ɛbaeɛ wɔ Abobɔda a ɛtɔ so dunsia (World War I) no, nkurasefoɔ no yɛe sɛ wɔnni nyɛ a ɛte sɛɛ no bio ɛda hɔ.
1884 mu no, Tesla kɔɔ Amerika Nsonsonhɔ Man mu na nya bo a ɛyɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ nipa a ɛyɛ din wɔ Edison Kompaani no mu New York City.
Ɔne kɔsoɔ Amerika sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ, na ɛnnaa pesewa anan, nkɔsoɔ abotan bi, na mmea a ɔdanee Charles Batchelor (ɔyɔkyerɛni wɔ ne asafo a edi kan mu) ka Thomas Edison kyerɛɛ no.
China ahenni no, wɔn akyiri yɛɛ sɛnea wɔde mfeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw ahyɛn; China te sɛ ɔman biara a na ɛwɔ apam, na ɛwɔ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ kɛseɛ.
Na ɛwom sɛnkyɛn ahorow no nso, wɛwɔ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ huam a manfoɔ no nyinaa yɛ pɛn so, na ɛda so asɛmpa. Ɛyɛ mfeɛ 60 a ɛwɔ Han afei nso Jin Dinasty hɔ no, na Three Kingdoms akyiri no na ɛyɛ den.
Ɛna mmere a ɛte sɛ̃ no, apam a ɛyɛ den kyɛn faa nobaa a wɔdeɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ sɛdeɛ no maa no.
Ɔkyeman Tuntum no kɛseɛ bio nti afeha a ɛyɛ den wɔ China manfoɔ sésɛmu a ɛyɛ mfeɛ dodoɔ no mu, adwuma a ɛyɛ den kɔɔ so maa mfeɛ pii na wusaa wɔn ho kyɛɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ sɛdeɛ wɔ Xi’an manpanin adumfoɔ no mu.
Wɔ mmoa a ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛ metric system din, abofra a ɛsi soafoɔ dwadie mu kɔ republikanism, ɔman a ɛyɛ den, na amane sɛ ɔman no yɛ mmaa a wɔwɔ hɔ no, ɛmfa mmaa biako pɛ a na ɛwɔ so.
Na ɛhwehwɛ a, abusuapanyin abɛyɛ sɛ yɛbɛyɛ mmeranteɛ biara a w’ani nte ase, na ama wɔn a wɔn nni nkɔmhyɛ a wɔn ho yɛ den a wɔte sɛ wɔbɛyɛ mmeranteɛ no nso no nya nkɔso.
Ɛyɛ sɛ nso ɛte sɛ abrafo no, efisɛ ɛno ara na ɛyɛ sɛ abrafo nnan a ɛwɔ hɔ no bedi dwuma na ɛyɛ sɛ wobɛboa no ma wɔn nnamso, na ɛyɛ sɛ wɔbɛboa no ma wɔn awooware.
Ɔsram a ɛne France so no, yɛe abofra maa mmoa a ɛwɔ nkurow biara a edi mu yɛɛ mfeɛ na wɔbɛyɛ nnamfoɔ a wɔdɔɔso a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔn akyi.
Muhammad na w’ani nnyaeɛ biara a ɛwɔ hɔ sɛnea ɛte sɛ saa yɛnni. Na ɔbɛyɛ adwuma sɛ ɔreba akopɔ a na ɛyɛ "Hira‘" wɔ "Noor" (hwere) mpoano mu ma ɔnhwehwɛ.
Ɔpenkuro no, a ɛhwehwɛɛ ahayɛsɛm yi, no maa w'adwuma pii sɛ Muhammad nhomaso a ɛyɛ den.
Mecca atifi agyapa a, abɔdeɛ no nyinaa asan nanso ɛyɛ mmerɛw wɔ wiase nyinaa mu.
Ɛnyɛ mmerɛw sɛ wuhu sɛ wose so akyɛ, na ɛnyɛ sɛ woanya yɛn no bio. Bere a wo redan hɔ no, woɖɔ wo ho akyɛ.
Ɛnyɛ nti sɛ woahe woho a, woanya saa asasea dɔɔse no na ɛyɛ sɛn sɛn a ɛwɔ soro ne nnwoma a ɛdehyɛ no. Ɛnyɛ den sɛ woanya ne woato woanim de, wo wɔ apam a mu.
Ɛyɛ Pyramid koro no a ɛwɔ Giza no na ɛyɛ mmerantɔw a ɛwɔ nnwɔtwe no mu bi a ɛte sɛe sɛ mmere a ɛyɛ ho a ɛbɛyɛ den kɔɔ soro.
Ɛyɛ Asamanfoɔ no demaa ɛhɔ, ɛka daa ɛsono mmienu no mu, Great Pyramid no yɛ nnhwima pii a wɔde baa anoma a wafa akyɛ akyi.
Giza Plateau no de, aane nso yɛde 'Giza Necropolis' na ɛwɔ Misré dwadiefóɔ adansé no mu, wodi pyramid dɔnko (dɛnkyɛma pyramid no yɛ kɛseɛ), mmoa dɔnko a ɛyɛ kɛseɛ, atɔbɔso dɔnko, ne Sphinx kɛseɛ.
Ɛyɛ sɛ piramidi no, a ɛyɛ den, na ɛboa ma Pharaoh Khufu, na piramidi kɛseɛ a ɛbɛyɛ kɛseɛ no, ntamgyin a ɛwɔ hɔ, ne nkyenkyɛn no de bɔɔ Khufu nyɛ, ne ne mma ne abusuafuo.
"Atɔe a ɛyɛ sɛ 'up bow' no yɛ sɛ 'V' na atɔe a ɛyɛ sɛ 'down bow' no nso yɛ sɛ abopon a ɛwɔ nkyɛn a ɛdɔ so."
Ɔsoro no kyerɛ sɛ wobɛfa abɔne no apam no so te, na wobɛtwa nea woafiri no. Ɔgyina hɔ no kyerɛ sɛ wobɛfa nkyɛn no (nea wo mankyɛfa abɔne no hɔ) so, na wobɛtwa abɔne no.
Ɛyɛ sɛ, sɛ wone fafo bow no, ɛma nsu a ɛnyɛ den sɛnea ɛte, nanso sɛ wone atuo bow no, ɛma nsu a ɛden den ma wɔhyia.
Wɔhyɛ no sɛ woanya wo nkyɛn sɛnkyɛn a, nanso hyɛ no sɛ nkyɛn a ɛyɛ din a ɛwɔ mmaa no wɔ akyerɛ sɛnea wo deba, enti ɛsɛ sɛ wo respekte koraa.
Ɔhene Kwesi Sesa a ɛyɛ sɛn pii, Afi Abena Marie Antoinette, mmoa a wɔn din de Marie Therese (ɔyɛ ɔbosam nnawɔtwe) ne Louis-Charles (ɔyɛ abɔdade nwɔtwe) ne Ɔhene no sisɛm, Abena Elizabeth, wɔ Ɔdaano Bosome no mmea ɛson, 1789, wosii wɔn tumi bɛyɛɛ Paris man mu firii Versailles, denkyem kyerɛwfo amanfoɔ nnan a na ɛyɛ adwoa paara bi nkyɛn.
Na wɔyɛɛ baa fam, wɔbɔɔ mpoano no de Paris, wɔn a manning a wɔdɔɔso abrantɛfoɔ te sɛ nnamfoɔ a na ɛyɛ ntam no, na ɛdɔɔso ma Kwame ne Abena Maame.
Abɔfra no tumi bi tumi akyerɛ Awulae ne Ahemaa kwan no nna akyɛ a, na wɔde nna no fata kɔ so.
Wɔ gyina so biara, nnipa a wɔyɛ anohyia no mu biara hwehwɛ Versaille manpanin a wɔde mmaa no kyee no agya wɔ abusuapanyin a ɔhyɛ ntena mu nav.
Amerika abrafo no abusuabusu a ɛyɛɛ sɛ Philippine manni no akyiri no, Philippinefo no ara a ɛyɛɛ nanso no nea ɛde ama no.
Na ɛhyiaa wɔn sɛ wɔhyɛ nnamda adwuma a Amerika anaa Amerika ababannefo aban no ne mmara mu, na ɛmaa nnamda a ɛyɛ den koraa ne nnamda a ɛwɔ amanɔne abotrɔ a Wall Street adwumayɛfo abotɔnkyekyɛ no din mu no ho mfa nkyere.
Ɛyɛ mpaapae, a, ɛno na ɛyɛ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den no mu, Philippinefo no de a wɔde ahwehwɛ no a, na ɛbɛyɛ Amerika so nteteɛ a ɛyɛ baako.
Templars nhyiamu a, wonya nea yɛbɛhyɛn sɛ́ wɔbɛyɛ biako no ntam akyi.
Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ, ahoteɛ a na ɛneɛ nkyekyɛm no too baa yɛ woɔ no, wɔfrɛ no 'High Middle Ages' – Europa manhyia nhyiaa a ɛwɔ mfeɛ mpɛn mmienu (AD 1000–1300) no mu.
Ɔbenkron Adwuma a Ɛhɔ a Ɛto so yɛɛ no, na Ɛyɛ mfa biara a edi kan no na ɛyɛ mfa biara a edi hɔ no, a ɛwɔ nhyeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ anaa 1500.
Teknologia abrabɔ ne nsɛm a ɛwɔ dodoɔ no, ɛfa dɔnkɔ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ hwehwɛ sɛ, teknoloji bɛyɛɛ sɛ yɛbɛhyia bio (technology-push) a na ɛyɛ mmeae sɛ yɛbɛhyia bio (technological imperative) kɔsi sɛ Ɛsono a ɛkeka teknoloji nsemmisa no biara nni dwuma abusuaba a ɛwɔ mmeaehwehwɛ a ɛyɛ sɛ teknoloji nhyehyɛe nyinaa yɛ den koraa wɔ abrabɔ ne amammerɛ mmara mu, na teknoloji nso w’ani gye asɛmpaka a ɛwɔ abom, ɛno nso yɛ den koraa ne mmea so yɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛ ne amammerɛ mu yɛde.
Yɛbɛyɛ sɛ, sɛnea wobɛyɛ a, nnwuma a ɛyɛ nwanwa no, w’akyiri koraa na ɛma nkyɛn biara a ɛto so abue.
Nanso, nnwomto a ɛyɛ sɛ Ghana nyinaa ma nkontaa no nni afa mu, enti yɛyɛɛ mfiase ahorow a ɛma nkontaa abubu no yɛ mmerɛw.
Mmoa a ɛyɛ sɛ yɛn nyinaa de nnwom kwan so, na ɛma nnwomto a ɛyɛ nwonwa no yɛ den kɛseɛ, a ɛkyɛn kyere sɛ yɛyɛ mfonini foforo wɔ aburokyerɛ mu de kɔmaa mmusuma a atwam.
Romanticism no ntam biara nnye nnamso yɛdenkyɛm a edi mũ bre a ɛyɛ sɛ Goethe, Fichte, na Schlegel mmea no hyɛn.
Ɛwɔ Romanticism ntam, apɔn a ɛwɔ hɔ no ne mmɔfra a ɛwɔ hɔ no hyiaa, na bere biara nnamfoa na abrabɔ a ɛwɔ apɔn no nyinaa bɛsii, na ɛte sɛnea obiara de, ɛyɛ mmerɛ bio sen sɛ yɛbɛhyɛ mmeaeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛ a yɛde bɛsii so.
Yɛdeɛ sɛ Paris no, ɛyɛ moda a ɛyɛ din pɛpɛpɛpɛ sɛ asɛmpasɛm a ɛwɔ wiase nyinaa so, ɛdeɛ sɛ Constantinople nso wɔtaa yɛn no sɛ asɛmpasɛm a ɛwɔ abusuapanyin Europa so.
Ɔbaa a ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛyɛ adwuma pa ara saa no fii ase ɛno na ɛto so de, ɛna ɛwɔ hɔ kosi bre a ɛyɛ mfe ahanumɔ ne ahano no.
Ɛdwin a ɛyɛɛ sɛ, abrabɔ bosompra a ɛhɔ no hyɛɛ ase ase wɔ afe dunsia kɔɔ dunsia no mu, esɛ sɛ nnaa ahwɛfo a na ɛbɛsɔreɛ wɔn nsa no sɛnea ɛyɛɛ, na nnaa wɔde abrobeɛ a ɛyɛ denkyem, ne mmea a ɛyɛ mmoa a ɛyɛ denkyem akyɛ no, na nnaa ɛyɛɛ deɛ wɔpɛ wɔ Byzantine kuw.
Naa ɛyɛ mfeɛ no, na Constantinople abusuapanyin din a ɛyɛ Fashion Mantam no kyɛɛ Paris.
Gothic din no yɛɛ dwan no akyiri mfe ahanan, mfe ahankron ne mfe ahanan nson.
Abɔdeɛ no mu nnaanom a edi kan no, ɛyɛɛ Byzantium asɛmfua no a ɛwɔ apueɛ fam no ho ban.
Nanso, nna εkwan a εyε yɛ bεhyia no yɛ yɛn ara, nsua a εwo hafi wosow a ɛwɔ wiase no te sɛ ɔyɛwɔ no mu nkyɛn no fii ase pɛpɛɛpɛ 25 kosi 30 afa.
Abatoɔ a ɛto so dodoɔ no, Europa anaafo bɛyɛɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ mfoniniwo ahorow a ɛyɛ wɔn ho. Crusades akyi, mmaa na wɔbɛfa botae sɛ ehyɛn mfonini.
Ntafoforo yɛdeɛ no nti sɛ wɔyɛ fam bi a w’anya nnwa a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ fam no na wɔn mmoa no de n’ani gyina hɔ no.
Nnwompa a yɛde hyɛ nnamsoɔ no yɛ mfiase, berepɔ no nso yɛ biako a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, na ɛtaa yɛ bio pii sɛnea ɛte so, na yɛfa nnamsoɔ a ɛwɔ fie a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛreɛ no bio, na yɛkyekyɛ nnamsoɔ foforoɔ ma ɛma yɛnya yɛn ara.
Abɛyɛ sɛ, ɛhɔ sɛnea farmer no nyinaa dɔ yɛɛ nkwantuo nwoma na ɛyɛ mmaa biara na ɛte sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ ama aman a ɛyɛ mmoa dɔɔso no nyinaa.
Subcultures no nyinaa hyɛ denkyɛm a yɛte ase wosane wɔn a adwuma a ɛyɛ den no, na ɛma wɔn ​​nya mmoa no bio sɛ wobɛyɛ sɛnea wo te.
Mmea a ɛwɔ subcultures no nte sɛe yɛbɛyɛ bi, ɛte sɛ wɔn din mu yɛ, wɔn nnam, nnamforo, wɔn wurae, na ɛwɔ hɔ bi a wɔwɔ hɔ no nti.
Nnɛmmere a ɛhyia subculture sɛ yɛyɛ biakɔ no, ɛte sɛ asɛmpone, nsemmwine, nkyimlin, aban, adwuma, apɔn, te sɛn, a na ɛyɛ no deɛ.
Mmea a ɛwɔ subculture bi mu no, wɔn a wɔboa wɔn ho sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ bi ara, wɔde mienu kɔkɔɔ, nnwuma, ne kasa foforo a wɔde di dwuma sɛ mmeae a wɔhyia mu.
Yɛdeɛ biara a yɛfa so ma obiara sɛnea sosodɔyɛ fa bi yɛ bɛhyia, ɛyɛ sɛ yɛboa afiri pa ara a wɔn akyi, anwummere, anigye, anaa nsemmisa a ɛfa nnamso a ɛwɔ mfeɛ no, wɔnna nnipa de ma wɔn anansesɛm na wɔteɛ wɔn mu.
Mmerew a ɛte sɛnea ha no, yɛfrɛ no "abofra a ɛyɛ dɔ" nyɛl, anaasɛ "abofra a ɛyɛ yɛnkyɛ". Bio, obiara a ɛyɛ dɔ a wɔatumi de no hyɛ nkurow no, wɔde no kae wɔn ananmu (te sɛ ne mma a wɔwoo no). Nnyɛ, medaase, nkyɛnkyɛn a wɔhwehwɛ abofra a w’ani ayɛ huam no, a wɔn ho yɛ den na wɔwɔ mmerɛw a ɛnyɛ yiye a anaasɛ abofra a w’apirekyɛ no na emu yɛ den no ne nti na wɔhwere no.
Mma a ɛyɛ adwuma a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a wɔde abotɔn a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛnne, anomaa a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛnne, a wɔgye di no wɔ wiase a wɔhwehwɛ nea wɔyɛ no a wɔhwehwɛ no a wɔhwehwɛ no a wɔhwehwɛ no. **More natural/common phrasing (preferred):** Mma a wɔde kɔsɔɔ so a wɔn a wɔwɔ hɔ no, anomaa a wɔde kɔsɔɔ so, bɛyɛ sɛ wɔde ma no wɔ wiase a wɔhwehwɛ nea wɔyɛ no a wɔhwehwɛ no a wɔhwehwɛ no. **Explanation of choices and nuances:** * **"Feral children"**: Translating "feral" directly isn't common in Twi in this context. I've used "mma a ɛyɛ adwuma a ɛyɛ mmerɛw" (children who live wild/in a difficult situation) or "mma a wɔde kɔsɔɔ so" (children who have been left to their own devices/abandoned). The latter is more idiomatic. * **"Severe child abuse or trauma"**: This is rendered as "abotɔn a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛnne, anomaa a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛnne" (serious hardship/suffering/abuse, serious trauma). * **"Before being abandoned or running away"**: "Wɔgye di no wɔ wiase" means "they left them in the world" (abandoned them). "Wɔhwehwɛ nea wɔyɛ no" (they sought something they did) is a general way to say "running away" - implying they were looking for a different life. The repetition of “wɔhwehwɛ no” is for emphasis, common in Twi. The second version is the more natural way a Twi speaker would express this complex thought.
Kɔn akyiri sɛ ɛsono no de bɛyɛɛ adwuma, na ɛsono nso de yɛɛ adwuma. Bio nso, ɛte sɛ ɔha bi na ɛwɔ hɔ a na ɛte sɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛɛ sɛ wɔde awo wɔ wiase mu a ɛyɛ ama won a na won nso na ɛwɔ hɔ bi a na ɛte sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛɛ ase wɔ wiase mu wɔn ho fi.
Ɛha yɛnkyi sɛ, sɛ yɛkyerɛ abusua a ɛnni ha no mu no, akyiri panyin no bebree biara, na ɛhwehwɛ ne mmoa a ɔkyerɛw no ho nhyeɛ no, te sɛ n’ani gye nkuraseɛ a ɛyɛ mmoa no, anaa n’ani atumi nnye nkuraseɛ a ɛyɛ mmoa no ho ase.
Nanso, sɛ project din a yɛyɛ no na ɛma nkyɛmu a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛnya nkɛntɛn so, na scaffolding no kyerɛ sɛ ɛne no nso ɛyɛ den kɛse.
Ɛyɛ sɛ scaffolding no yɛɛ mfaso sɛnea yɛboa afoforo te sɛ sɛ wɔboa no a wɔyɛ nneɛma foforo anaa wɔde komputa programa foforo abɛyɛ, ɛno nso yɛɛ mmeaeɛ sɛnea yɛboa no nyinaa.
Abɔdeɛ a wɔde hyɛ nnamso biara te sɛ ɛyɛ mmoa ne ɛyɛ nanso, wobɛkyerɛ sɛ nea ɔkyerɛkyerɛni no te sɛ abɔdeɛ a wɔde hyɛ nnamso no, na ɛsono Microsoft Office man biara nso te sɛ no.
Ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn a ɛwɔ software mu no, wɔde bɛyɛ sɛ wɔbɛhu adeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, wobɛtumi nkyɛ mu, na wobɛboa afi aseɛ a ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɔkwankyɛfo bɛtena ase yɛn ho bio.
Mmoa a ɛwɔ hɔ no de bɛyɛ mfeɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ bi, wɔde abofra a ɛyɛ den no kwan so, efisɛ wɔn a wɔn ho yɛ nnyɛ, abusua no, a na ɛwɔ hɔ nso.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw a onipa biara akyɛ pɛn na ɛnyɛ deɛ ɛyɛ nwandan, nyansa koro no, na ɛte sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ.
Yɛte ase wɔ foster care abrabɔfo no sɛ abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ mma wɔn a ɛhwehwɛn.
Aban no a yɛde bɛma mmoa a ɛsono so, agyefo a w’anya dɔ, sukuu a ɛte sɛ nsuo, ne abusuabɔ a ɛyɛ yiye.
Aban a wɔde abɔfra a wɔayɛ sɛ wɔnya nkwan so, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔnya nneyɛe a ɛna nea na ɛwɔ hɔ a wɔde sii hɔ bio.
Anetapere kyekyere mass communication ne interpersonal communication nyina biara.
Internɛtɛ no ntamgyinafoɔ ne nneɛma a ɛyɛ mfiase yɛ mmeaeɛ a ɛde ma yɛn nyinaa abɛyɛ mfidwuma ne abɔdeɛ so adwuma no.
Mɛkyerɛ sɛ, "nsusua" ne "nnamfoɔ a yɛtaa yɛ" a ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ ɛyɛ mmerɛwbea a ɛyɛ ma obiara a ɔde ma Internɛt yɛ (James et al., 1995).
Eighmey ne McCord (1998) akyerɛkyerɛe sɛ, nneɛma a yɛte sɛ yɛbɛyɛ ho nimdeɛ a ɛyɛ mmera ne abusuabusuabɔ a ɛda nso yɛ nneɛma a ɛhyɛ ma nnamfokrow a wɔde yɛnkyereɛ website ahorɔw a wɔn a wɔhwɛ so no dema.
Vidio asɛm a yɛde bɛyɛ sɛnea yɛte ase hwehwɛ no, ɛmaa yɛahu nhoma a ɛkyerɛ sɛnea nna a ɛyɛ denkyɛm, nna a ɛwɔ hɔ anaa ɛtwa ayɛ sɛ mfe few pii no, wɔ hyɛ no nsɛm.
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛhyia bio, ɛte sɛnea yɛte ase hyɛ sɛ obi bɛte ase w'asɛm a, yɛkyere sɛ wobɛhwehwɛ nsenseneɛ a ɛwɔ ne te sɛne no ho na yɛahu sɛ onnim.
Oliver Sacks, nhoma a edi kan so, "Ɔhene no Ɔsram," mu no, kyee sɛ nnaa yɛn a w’ani nnye abotire adwuma a ɛyɛ sɛ w’ani ayɛ denkyem koraa no, nanso maame biara a wɔn ho nhye agyina hɔ ma wɔbɛkyere sɛ ɛyɛ yiye.
Ɔde abrabɔ fa sɛ mfaso sɛnea yɛte sɛe nnamfoɔ no ho no, nso na ɛbɛyɛ sɛ aduru a ɛyɛ sɛn no, te sɛ abɔ a yɛdɔn no nso, wɔn nso wɔ w’abrabɔ a wɔfa so.
Ɛtɔ so dwumase a ɛwɔ mfeɛ mpem mmienu no nyinaa ayɛ sɛ wɛwɔ mmea a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu: a ɛsra ne a ɛyɛ mfiase.
Mmutasyon hyɛ DNA mu nhwɛso foforo, na nneɛma a ɛyɛ yiye no taa bɔ abɔntɔn a ɛwɔ mmaa na ɛtumi sɛ wɔde besi so.
Abusuadwuma ne mmara nhyehyɛε a ɛyɛ den ma mfaso no akyi ne mma mu, abusuadwuma a ɛyɛ den ne mmara nhyehyɛε a ɛyɛ den ma mfaso no akyi ne mma mu, daa biara.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛ, sɛ wɔwɔ savanna no so a, abofra bi a n'nni dwadwa yɛ sɛ yɛn no, ɛyɛ nnyɛ sɛ ɔbɛfa nnwuma a ɛwɔ abotabotan no mu no ara de hyɛ n'adwuma amino-acid a ɛde ma no.
Akyiri sɛ woammɔ woakyere no, ɛwɔ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ den: ntutu a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, ahyia, na ɛda so ara nso, wutuo.
Akwantuo a ɛyɛ mfeam no, protein a ɛwɔ abrafo ne mmea a ɛyɛ mfeam no ara na ɛyɛ mfeam, nanso ɛbɛyɛ sɛ yɛsiesie no bio na ɛyɛ mfeam ma yɛn, te sɛ yɛn a yɛ primate.
Ɛte sɛnea ɛte biara, nsem a yɛde hyɛ nanso (dɛdɛɛ, apɔnɔ, kookoo) ɛnyɛ denkyem, na ɛma yɛhu protein kɛseɛ a ɛwɔ nsammua biara a yɛte sɛe.
Nyɛ yɛahyɛ no nyinaa akyi, ɛno ara yɛnnhwehwɛn sɛ yɛn nnanom a ɛhyɛn no nso de ahenni no bɛyɛ pɛn sɛ yɛbɛteaseɛfo a ɛwɔ savana no te sɛnea ɛte anaa.
Nnipa a wɔyɛ mfaaseɛ no mu yɛɛ sɛ wɔdwo na wɔsesaa wɔn ho akyi, na akyiri no, wɔbɔ abusuafɔ wɔ mfeɛ mpem akyi (10–60 mfeɛ).
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛ wo bɛyɛ saa no na woanya nkwa nketewa a ɛnnyɛ den kyerɛ sɛ wo hwehwɛ a ɛnnye wo ntam no koraa, na mmɛn woahu afiri.
Ɛna woa te sɛ wote a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ den sɛ woa bɛyɛ ntam no, woapue koraa no akyiri wo bedi so na woantumi nnyɛ wo nna ano ama woakyiri no akyiri woahu. **(Alternative, slightly more concise version):** Ɛna woa te sɛ wote a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ den sɛ woa bɛyɛ ntam no, yɛmma no awiei koraa wɔ hɔ, na ɛma wo hu die a wo bɛkɔ so yɛ no ase.**
Ɛbinom a ɛwomа biorhythm din no nso kyerɛ sɛ wo de hyerew a ɛyɛ dɔ (dɛnkyɛm pɛn na anoma a ɛyɛ mpatapɔ) a ɛyɛ awoowɔ kɔɔ mfiase, na ɛma wo tumi abuburo de kɔɔ hwee.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea wobɛhyia abotabata a ɛwɔ wo mu no, na nea ɛkɔ so ara wɔ mprɛteɛ no, ɛyɛ sɛnea wo nnyigyei ne wo honhom kɔ so no.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wubɛyɛ mmerɛ bio, na ɛyɛ mmerɛ pa ara. Ɔbarima biara wɔ dwan sɛ ɔbɛboa afa abusuabɔ ne adɔso.
Ɛte sɛnkyɛn panyin ara na ɛbɛyɛ sɛnea yɛbɛhu kwan kɔ ntam. Ɛdenam adwuma a yɛtaa hu a, ne adwuma a yɛtaa hu no nti na yɛbɛhyiaa ntam.
Buddha adesua no na ɛde Tibetan Buddhism no yɛ, a na Mahayana nhyira nhyehyɛe ne Indian Yoga no nso ne mmoa a ɛde no yɛe.
Ɛyɛ sɛ, mprempren Tibetan Buddhism no yɛ mmoa. Ɛwɔ Kundalini Yoga, mmedua ahorow, na nea wotumi de yɛ nyinaa hyia no.
Kundalini Yoga no, Kundalini ngyinam (nnyansramma ngyinam) yoga nnananɔm, hwɛso, mprɛbɛ, mantra ne nkyigyaa mu na ɛyɛ yɛn mma.
Tibetan mmeduaa mfinfini no ne Ɔbraa Yoga. Ɔbraa ahorow a yɛhyɛ no no nkyekyɛmu akyɛ sɛnea nna nna, nna a ɛwom no na ɛyɛ yɛn, na ɛma yɛnya wo mma.
Germany na ɛyɛɛ adɔn wɔ Mpɔtam hwehwɛ a ɛto so aba, na ɛmaa USSR ne USA bɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ. Nanso, sɛ hwehwɛ no fii aseɛ no, ɛsom a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, abrabɔ, na mmeba a ɛyɛ denkyɛm, na ɛmaa nsan biara nnyɛ mmeaba.
Ɔda akyiri sɛ yɛdeɛn no nyinaa akyi mfe abuan no, nnaa ɛhyehyɛfo no yɛɛnkyɛkyɛm a ɛeɛ sɛ Cold War sii hɔ.
Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɛbɛda so abɔnten 40 a ɛyɛ sɛ yɛbɛyɛ nhyira, yɛbɛyɛ sɛ yɛbɛyɛ nhyira na ama afoforo ayɛ yɛn ho nhyira, wɔn a yɛde ma wɔn, wɔ abusuapɔn afã a ɛyɛ Afrika kɔ Asia, Afghanistan, Cuba ne bɔne a ɛyɛ nso.
Ɔbɛnem 17, 1939 no, Poland aban a ɛyɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ adwuma no yɛe dɔɔso a, na ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ wɔbɛtena hɔ na ɛbɛsan ayɛ mfeɛsɛ wɔ Romania apemfa a ɛwɔ asubɔnten no so.
Nanso, ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛnea, nnhyɛmma akyiri no no gyawu koraa biara, te sɛ daa biara, bere a sɛnkyɛmu no, abɔdin deɛ ɛto so 800,000 a ɛwɔ Soviet Union Red Army mu no bɛhyia Poland atifi fam no, wɔn a wɔde yɛɛ Belarus ne Ukraine mfronto akyiri no, wɔn a wɔkyerɛkyerɛ Riga Apam Nhyehyɛma, Soviet-Poland Annsɔn Nhyehyɛma, ne nkyem ahorow biara a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ pɛpɛpɛpɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ no ho.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛnea ɛyɛ yɛyɛ sɛ wɔfa nkontontoɔ dekyɛ abɔdeɛ a ɛso te sɛ nnamfo ne nnaano kyɛn akyiri nnwompa ho.
Ná asɛmpapan a navyfoɔ no di nka sɛ yɛbɛyɛ bɛn no, ɛyɛ sɛ wobɛyɛ sɛ w’nkyɛn a ɛyɛ kwan ma w’nini ne nneɛma na ɛde kɔ so, na nna sɛ w’atɔfoɔ no nso w’ani bɛhyia w’nini ne nneɛma kɔ so.
Ɔkwan so te sɛnea edi kan no, nea ɛyɛ den koraa wɔ mfeɛ akyiri yi mu no, na ɛyɛ Asase-Mantam no ahyɛnso a edi kan wɔ Hwehwɛ Hwehwɛ II mu. Amerikani no ne wɔn tumi biara ne nsaakye biara na ɛwom sɛ wɔbɛkyere mpoano so akyiri Atlantik Manfoɔ no sɛnea wɔbɛboa Britania.
Ɛwom sɛnkyɛn no, agodie a ɛyɛ mmeranteɛ, na ɛwɔ U-boats mu no, na ɛte sɛnea wɔbɛhyia ɔsram no.
Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ Allies nobaa akyerew no, Germany bɛte sɛnea ɛyɛɛ Europa no nyinaa so, na ɛbɛhyia Britain.
Abɔdeɛ a ɛte sɛ sɛ wɔhyɛɛ nkyɛnkyɛnii a ɛyɛ sɛ mfeɛ 10,000 akyi ara wɔ Iran man mu Zagros Mountains no.
Ɔkokɔɔ a ɛyɛ mfeɛ pii ne nnhyɛsoɔ no fii ase ayɛ nneɛma a ɛyɛ mfeɛ pii no de, na ɛwom sɛ wosoo nimdeɛ a ɛyɛ mfeɛ pii a wɔde susu nwanwa, tɛsɛ, nnam, ne apɔn.
Abɔdeɛ adepa a ɛwɔ hɔ no, wɔtaa de wɔn bɛyɛ abɔdeɛ a ɛte sɛ nnwa a ɛtaa yɛnnyɛ wɔ apam, afoturo kwan so, ne nea ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn a wɔde wɔn anaa abɔfrɛ a ɛyɛ mmoa, te sɛ nea yɛteɛ yɛnnyɛ sɛ ɔbɔfo. Ɛdeɛ biara a ɛyɛ awoowɔ no, wɔde pɛpɛɛpɛpɛ a ɛyɛ mfi biara di yɛn.

Berebi wagonways no nwereɛ faakyereɛ biara nanso, na ɛmaa aburokyereɛ a na ɛde na yɛn ho akyi no boa wɔn kɔ so dɔn sen na wɔgye nsoa a ɛyɛ mmerɛw bio a na ɛwɔ saa berɛ no.
Aponkyeɛ ahorow bi a yɛde bɛma apon a ɛwɔ so no na yɛyɛeɛ no ​​mprɛmprɛm. Nanso, ɛyɛ mfeɛ sɛ apon no ​​bɛyɛ mfiasee sɛ ɛwɔ demire a ɛyɛ te sɛ mmaa a ɛwɔ soro no.
Ɛyɛɛ dwanma, nanso agya-dɔn no baa dɔn wiase a, w’ani yɛɛ mmerɛw no sɛee dɔn wɔ nnaanom a ɛyɛ mmaa a ɛwɔ hɔ no so.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛnea, nwanɛ a ɛyɛ nwene a ɛwɔ hɔ no na ɛyɛ hyɛn a ɛyɛ mmerɛ no. Afebɔso, 1767 mu no, na ɛkyɛ sɛnea a ɛyɛ mmerɛ pii a ɛto so abien.
Ɛyɛ mfe ahanan mu no, nnipa fii ase wɔn nwoma kɔ so, na Homo Erectus (wɔkyerɛ sɛ 'nnipa a w'akyiri so') bɛyɛ mfe abuan no dua mu no, na na nnipa fi ase kɔ so yɛ te sɛnea yɛte sɛden.
Medaase, ɛhyehɔ no, Australopithecusfo no na nnkae sɛ wɔbɛhyia bi ara yɛ adwuma wɔn akyi.
Ɛyɛ adwuma a ɛkyerɛ sɛ abubu a ɛwɔ Australopithecus nnhunu a ɛyɛ sɛ yɛwoo no afi 4.2-3.9 milion afa ahyia no, nanso Sahelanthropus bɛyɛ sɛ wuhuu sɛ wosii nna no saa ara ansa ɛyɛ mfe apem aduokrono no.
Yɛte sɛ yɛboa ama abɔdeɛ no, yɛte sɛ yɛkɔ so di dwuma wɔ abɔdeɛ so dwuma a ɛyɛ mmeranteɛ no mu, na yɛte sɛ yɛbɛyɛ abotɔn a ɛyɛ sɛ yɛhyɛ nnaawɔtweɛ a ɛreba nnaawɔtweɛ no koraa so.
Ɛyɛ sɛ ɛte sɛ mprempren no a yɛde yɛ mfease pii mu. Nanso, sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ yɛnya mfiase a ɛnyɛ deɛ yɛde bɛtumi ahyia mfease koraa no a, yɛbɛsua nnamso a ɛma nnyansahyɛfo no, na yɛbɛhyia afi ase.
Ɛyɛ dɛn na ɛte sɛ ɔhaw ahorow a, adwumam no ayɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ den brea nyinaa enti brea yɛn ara nnamɔ ne teknolo gyidi ahorow, na nnamɔ nhyeɛ a ɛyɛ den no nso ayɛ mmerɛw brea yɛn ntam nim nteɛ, efisɛ yɛn nnipa dɔ no ara ne yɛn ho adwuma a yɛde ma den koraa.
Ɛna akyiri sɛ Congress de abubu no sɛ mmere pa wɔ Ɔbɛnimma Bosia no mu a, wosii nkyerew no, a Ɔbenfo a na ɛwɔ Congress, John Hancock ne Agyapade Charles Thomson dii kan, akyiri a wɔde baa nkyekyɛ a ɛwɔ John Dunlap abɔde mu no.
Ɔdaadaa biara a ɛtɔ so 150 kosi 200, na wɔyɛ kwan so, ɛyɛ "Dunlap broadsides" a yɛte sɛe.
Abofra a ɛyɛ sɛn no a na John Nixon de yɛɛ no, na ɛyɛ sɛn no a ɛyɛ mmoa no a ɛyɛ Independence Hall ase so, wɔ Ɔbɛnimmaa 8 no.
Ɔde aboafo bi ahyɛ George Washington wɔ Ogyefuo bosome no mu a ɛto so 6, na ɔde akyerɛkyerɛ adɔnkɔ so wɔ New York wɔ Ogyefuo bosome no mu a ɛto so 9. Aboa a ɛyɛ kwan no nyaa London wɔ Ɔbɔbɔn bosome no mu a ɛto so 10.
Ɛyɛ sɛ, abisa a ɛtɔ so 25 a Dunlap ahyɛ ase no, ɛno na ɛyɛ mfonini a edi kan a ɛwɔ hɔ a yɛahu afi ma saa nkyerɛkyerɛ no. Akyirikyiri a ɛdɔ so no nni hɔ bio.
Ɔsono paara a ɛwɔ mmeaɛ sɛnea ɛte no, wosusu sɛ nnhunu anum a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛne dino soro no na ɛwɔ hɔ a ɛte sɛ ɛyɛ mmoa. Yɛfrɛ no nsua.
Aane nnanom no yɛn nni hɔ a yɛde dino saw sɔre, ɛfie no ne nsa koraa wɔn a wɔn a wɔmfa wɔn ho ahyɛ ase.
Sɛnea ɛte sɛ, ɛwɔ dɔnkoɔ a ɛyɛ sɛ onipa de woho a, ɛwɔ nso nneyɛɛ a ɛkeka dɔnkyɛm a ɛte sɛ dinosaur.
Wɔn nsaeɛ ne asikyire twa, wɔde kwan te, na wɔteɛ wɔn mfinfin mmienu akyiri sɛ T-Rex.
Ɛte sɛnea komputa didi ara a ɛde yɛ den kyerɛ sɛ wɔhwehwɛ nea ɛkyerɛ sɛ nnommmerɛ a ɛyɛ mmiɛn ne nnwɔtwi a wɔde boa ma nneɛma a yɛde bɛyɛ sɛnea yɛyɛ de.
Number a ɛyɛ binary no nea ɛbɛboa no biara yɛ sɛ 0 anaa 1, na yɛfrɛ nneɛma a ɛwɔ hɔ no binary digits – a ɛyɛ bits wɔ komputa kasa mu.
Mpoison a ɛwɔ hɔ no nni saa ara a ɛte sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ biara a wobetumi de hu no. Nsonson, sɛnea ɛte biakoa na ɛyɛ sɛnkyi, ɛnyɛ sɛ wobetumi de hu nkyere no gu akyiri yi.
Mepɔn a ɛyɛ sɛnea wobɛkyerɛ mu no, sɛ wosusu sɛ woyi yare a ɛwɔ nna bi mu anaa nsuo a ɛyɛ huam a ɛwɔ fie mu no, ɛyɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛso tẽẽ sɛ woyaa yare a ɛyɛ huam.
Kyekye ne te sɛn a ɛwɔ hɔ no so, na woahu sɛnea wobɛyɛ faa a ɛde baa yɛn anim na ɛyɛ yɛn ho akyi.
Entomologfoɔ no de ‘bug’ din no yɛ denkyemmaa nhyeɛ wɔn a yɛaka nkyeneɛ deɛ, saa mmoa a ɛyɛ mmea a ɛwɔ nkontonkron no.
Ɛsɛm no fi aseɛ wɔ apam a yɛde bɛhyɛn Bed-bugs so, ɛyɛ nkyɛn a wɔde yɛn ho mfa ho.
Mpemba a ɛyɛ sɛnkyireɛ ne mpemba a ɛyɛ mmea, ɛsono wɔ mpesa a ɛwɔ hɔ a wɔde bɛn a wɔbɛhyia wɔ mu no.
Ɔman Amerika no nyina so, Multiple Sclerosis (MS) asase a ɛte sɛnea ɛyɛ no, ɛyɛ no sɛ 400,000 akyiri yi, na ɛyɛ mmea na mmusuma a ɛyɛ den no mu no, sɛnkyɛn nanso mmea a ɛyɛ den no nyina so.
MS yareɛ no yɛ mmerɛw a ɛtaa yɛ central nervous system no, a ɛwɔ apam a ɛyɛ sɛ brain, spinal cord, na optic nerve.
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛ no ne sɛ, abofrafo no mmea mmaa adwuma a ɛyɛ den no dwoma biara mu no, mmabarima no asɛm no mu nkyem ahorow no te sɛ abien.
Abusuakuma bi betumi akyerɛ sɛ ɛnyɛ wo deɛ wo te sɛɛ, anaa wo abofra deɛ wo te sɛɛ, sɛ wobɛyɛ adwuma biara nni dwuma.
Mmeaeɛ a ɛte sɛnea enti pɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nwanini nhyehyɛe afiri sɛ wɔn paapa a wɔnni.
Abanndwom mu no, woaferɛ a wɔwoo no no na ɛma wɔn ntam adwuma a ɛde baa fam, na afei mmaa bi a wɔbɛyɛ abusuafuo no bɛyɛ mmoa a wɔwoo no no.
Nkyerɛkyerɛ no deɛ, sɛ́deɛ ɛyɛ a ɛtaa nyinaa so yɛ sɛ yɛhu sɛ obiara te sɛnea asase yi yɛ bɛn no, ɛyɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛyɛ dɛnkyɛma. Ɛdeɛ yɛyɛ no nso na ɛhwehwɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ ahorow biara a ɛyɛ dɛnkyɛma.
Ɛnyɛ sɛ ɔyɛ den koraa deɛ, nanso nsesa, na nsesa no nso yɛ mprehuru a ɛyɛ sɛ wohuu biribi a ɛba fam akyi, sɛ wubetumi abue kyere no. Ɛdeɛ sɛ wotua adwuma so, woahwehwɛ ne woho ahyia nso na ɛhyɛ daasefo asuafoni.
Ɔdayɛfo ne abofrafo nobaa abɛyɛ mfiridwuma a ɛwɔ asɛmpaka ahorow ne, wɔn a wɔwɔ hɔ no, Bible a ɛwɔ Latini mu no.
Aristotle nkyereyɛ ahorɔw a ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte so, na ɛwɔ mmea a ɛyɛ den koraa a, akyiri kɔɔ psychology nso.
Berebiara a ɛkyerɛ sɛ Greek kasa no hyɛɛ ase, Weso no teeɛ sɛ wɔayɛ mfiase wɔ Greek mmoa ne sɛnedwa so.
Ɛsono ahanan a ɛwomɔ so ahorow ne mfasoɔ mpo a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛte sɛe no, som sɛ ɛde besi ma obiara sɛ wɔwɔ mfeampɛn a ɛwɔ hɔ bio ne wɔn a wɔyɛ biohɔ ma wɔn akyi.
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛahu sɛnea nnaano a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛnyɛ deɛ ɛma yɛnya abrabɔ mu fi nnaano a ɛwɔ nnaano mu no, wɔapɛ sɛ yɛahu wɔn wɔ nnamfo nyinaa mu, a na ɛwɔ mmea, fungi, apam, na nnwuma a ɛte sɛ nea ɛyɛ a ɛwɔ mmea nyinaa mu.
Ɛhɔ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ n’apɔn no yɛ mfiridwuma a ɛte sɛ ne ho a ɛbɛma wobue kwan no bio pɛpɛpɛpɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ no, ɛde biara nanso ɛno nso betumi ayɛ mfiridwuma bio ɛwom sɛ wanya nkɔso a ɛwɔ nnaanoo. **Explanation of choices & nuances:** * **Ɛhɔ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ n’apɔn no:** Literally "the place that is biological that is in the body". This establishes the concept of internal biological processes. "Apɔn" is used for body. * **yɛ mfiridwuma a ɛte sɛ ne ho:** "is a function that is like itself" - attempting to convey 'self-sustaining'. Twi often uses descriptive phrasing rather than single words for complex concepts. * **a ɛbɛma wobue kwan no bio pɛpɛpɛpɛpɛ:** "that will let you continue the cycle again and again". "Kwan" represents cycle or rhythm. "Bio pɛpɛpɛpɛpɛ" emphasizes the continuous nature. * **sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ no, ɛde biara nanso:** "as it will be, everything, but also..." - transitional phrase connecting the continuous cycling to the next clause. * **ɛno nso betumi ayɛ mfiridwuma bio ɛwom sɛ wanya nkɔso a ɛwɔ nnaanoo:** "it too can continue to function even if you don't get signals from the outside." "Nnaanoo" refers to the outside world, "nkɔso" are signals/cues. **Important Note:** Translating complex scientific concepts directly into Twi can be challenging. This translation prioritizes conveying the *meaning* accurately, even if it requires more descriptive phrasing than the original English. There might be other valid translations depending on the specific context and intended audience.
Hershey ne Chase ne nsesaadee a ɛyɛe sɛ́ DNA yɛ mmoa a ɛde ma wonya mmoa.

Ɔsono ne ahansia akyi, wɔn a wɔfrɛ no Aristarchus no kyerɛɛ sɛ asase so nna a ɛwɔ hɔ no hyɛ sɛnkyɛn no yɛn akyi.
Medaase, here's the Twi translation: **Adwuma a ɛte sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ no, abɛn a yɛn pɛ sɛ ɔwɔ hɔ a ɛyɛ yiye, nanso abɛn pii no nso nnaasi sɛ ɛyɛ te sɛ no, na ɛte sɛ ɔfrɛɛ planet no nyinaa, efiri akenkan a ɛyɛ sɛ Asase no na ɛkyerɛ mmaa a ɛwɔ hɔ no (na ɛwom sɛ ɔkyerɛ nso bintang a yɛwɔ hɔ no).** **Explanation of choices and nuances:** * **Adwuma a ɛte sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ no:** "The way things seemed/stood…" This sets up the context of differing opinions. * **abɛn a yɛn pɛ sɛ ɔwɔ hɔ a ɛyɛ yiye:** "Some people who we thought were right..." (lit. people that we liked that he was right) * **nanso abɛn pii no nso nnaasi sɛ ɛyɛ te sɛ no:** "But many people also believed the opposite..." (lit. people many also opposed that it was like that) * **na ɛte sɛ ɔfrɛɛ planet no nyinaa:** "...and they believed that the planets all..." * **efiri akenkan a ɛyɛ sɛ Asase no na ɛkyerɛ mmaa a ɛwɔ hɔ no:** "...revolved around the Earth..." (lit. coming from the thought/idea that Earth is the one that carries/shows the things/planets there) This phrasing uses 'kyerɛ' (to carry/show) in a way that depicts the Earth as the central body. * ** (na ɛwom sɛ ɔkyerɛ nso bintang a yɛwɔ hɔ no):** “…(and even the stars)” I have aimed for a natural and accurate translation, conveying the full meaning of the original English sentence. This is a complex idea, so the Twi sentence is correspondingly long and detailed.

Ɛyɛ sɛ yɛbɛhu wo ho sɛ keyboard no bɛbɔn biara sɛnea ɛbɛte sɛ ɛyɛ den koraa a ɛde ba.
Abom no de ahotosoɔ a ɛfa ho sɛ, sɛ wo de proton a ɛtee ne neutron a ɛtee kɔfa so a, ɛhyia sɛ wo yɛnna biribiara a ɛyɛ ahotosoɔ no.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wote nnwoma biara pii a woanya wo tum biako mmere biako so, na woakɔ so. Bio nso, sɛ wosuaa nnaa no mu yɛn pii a, woanya energy biara a ɛwɔ hɔ no bɛsɔre.
Monomolekyɔ ahorɔw biara w’ani nkyɛ a ɛma no nyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ ma no nya nkɛntɛn sɛnea wobɛhyia no.
Akwansrafo a ɛwɔ Osram ne mmerɛw a ɛyɛ mu. Agya no a ɛwɔ Osram no de akyerɛ sɛ 'crust'.
Akyiri no atɔeɛ no yɛ sɛ kilomita 70 fiehwe, na ne apam no yɛ kilomita 100 fiehwe.
Ɛyɛ hwee asempapa mu na ɛyɛ pɛ asempapa mu.
Maawo a, ɛbɛyɛ sɛ wɔnnum a ɛwɔ hwehwɛn no mu no te sɛ maria no, ɛyɛ den kɛse nti asase no nsoa a ɛyɛ hwee no te. Ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛ abɔde a ɛyɛ fɛre no bɛsɔre abɔ wo so.
Nnwomtoa a ɛkyerɛ sɛnea yɛte sɛe ahyɛ yɛn sɛnkyɛn no, na ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ yɛahu nea ɛma yɛn hwɛ kwan a yɛbɛpɛne no.
ɛsɛm a ɛwɔ hɔ no de akyerɛ sɛ nnamfo wɔ mmerɛ ne/anaasɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ bi a ɛte sɛɛ sɛ wɔabɔ wɔn ho ban na ɛsɔnso wɔn de kɔɔ mpaninfoɔ mu.
Sɛnkyɛm pii no ne bɛhyia mpaapaeɛ a ɛde ma nwonwa a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔnya nkyereɛ, na ɛdeɛ sɛ nwonwa a ɛwɔ hɔ a ɛbɛma wɔnya nkyereɛ anaa nni nkyereɛ.
Ahafo abrabɔ a ɛyɛ den no mmiɛnsa a ɛne Maslow nhyehyɛe a ɛfa mmoa no ne Hertzberg mmoa abrabɔ a ɛwɔ hwehwɛn no.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte biara, mienyɛ nnan a ɛte sɛnea mmamɛfo fi aseɛ hyehyɛase no. Ɛdɔɔso no, wɛyɛ sɛ wode bɛyɛ mienyɛ afrafra bi (ne maame a wɔyɛ mienyɛ afrafra).
Yɛbɛyɛ sɛ yɛnim manager yi nni nnamso nkyerɛkyerɛ asɛm a ɛnnye ho a, nnaano a ɛfa nnamso, nnamso kyekyɛ, abotrɛ a wɔde ama afoforo, na nnaano a wɔde hyɛ mmadwo ma wɔn asɛmpasɛm.
Ɛwom sɛnkyɛn no mu akyiri, onipa no bɛyɛ biako a wonnim no bio, na w'ani so sɛ ɔde bɛyɛ biako a ɛde ama ne ho na ama tim no nyinaa a ɛyɛ dɛn no.
Ɛnyɛ sɛnea ɛte biara, na ɛna koraa no nanso ɔsoafo no hyia mponkyim na ɔhyia mponkyim a ɛyɛ pɛnkyɛn no.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛnea no, sɛnea no nso ma abusuakuro ne ahenni no ntam kyekyɛ a ɛda so.
Mfiridwuma a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛboa no no, yɛsusu so dodoɔ a ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛpɛ wɔn sɛnea yɛboa firidwuma a ɛyɛ mmeranteɛ no, nanso ɛwɔ mmeranteɛ a yɛhuw.
Mmodɔm a wɔyɛ sɛnkyɛn no, wɔnim sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ abusuafɔ a wɔwɔ hɔ no ho sɛdeɛ.
Ɛsono wɔn a wɔyɛ asɛmpae a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔn timtim no nso bɛyɛ sɛnea wɔte sɛ wɔbɛhyia bio a ɛkyerɛ sɛ nnyigyi a ɛwɔ nkurow a wɔn apamfo no nni hwee ase.
Nyansafoɔ mienu a ɛyɛ sɛnea Larson ne LaFasto (1989, p109) kyerɛ no, a nea ɛwɔ hɔ no, ɛyɛ virtual team deɛn a ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ.
"Abofra biara ne nimdeɛ a wɔde ma no, na ɛyɛ abusuapanyin a ɛde hyɛ ma no. Abofra biara nimdeɛ a ɛde hyɛ ma no no na ɛmaa nnamso a ɛde ma wɔn nyinaa."
Ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛbɛhyia biara bɛte sɛn na wanya nte sɛ nnaahunu bi a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛde baa yɛbɛyɛ nhyehyɛse kuo? Ɔkwan a ɛyɛ sɛ yɛbɛhyia nhyehyɛse kuo no nyinaa mu nyɛ, na ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛ yɛbɛyɛ so. Ɛyɛ mfeamu a ɛtaa ba no mu biara a yɛtaa hyɛ no nsɛm a, na ɛyɛ mmerɛw ɛyɛ so.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a atwa ho a ɛwɔ ntamgyinafoɔ abaguan no nyinaa so dabi, na yɛbɛtumi abɔ wo hɔ ma nnamɔne ne mmeranteɛ ayɛ yiye.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛ a, sɛ abɔde ahorow biara hyɛn mpae a, wɔhyɛ ne ho sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ bi ara, ɛtaa fa biako bema abɔde no ato nsuo, na ɛmaa wɔbɛyɛ mmeaeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛ a ɛtaa de ma asɛmpasɛni no deɛ ɛyɛ yɛn ho.
Abofra biara sɛnea yɛbɛyɛ mfonini no, yɛn nanamfoɔ de bɛyɛ mfonini kwan, nanso ne nyinaa yɛte asempa a yɛahu dɔm, na yɛn apam no nso.
Angel (2006) de akyerɛ sɛ, Kontiniwom nhyehyɛe no yɛ nea ɛyɛ sɛ yɛnhyehyɛfoɔ no nkɔsoɔ so te sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ biara mu yɛdenkyem a ɛboa amammɔfoɔ sɛ wɔbɛnya nnuan no mu abre.
Nnwonkyerɛ ne nnamfoa a ɛkyerɛ n'akora so a ɛma yɛhu biako sɛnea yɛte sɛe nensa no. Ɛyɛ mfiase yɛn nnoom ayɛ mfiase pii ma yɛayɛ mpaapae.
Akyiri a ɛwom sɛnkyerɛ a ɛwɔ nna a ɛyɛ sɛnkyerɛ ne nnwuma, ɛma abɔdeɛfo nya abusuabɔ wɔ mmesua mu.
Ɛyɛ denam ahofadi sɛ yɛakyiri biara a ɛne honam, abotire, ntaba, ne asu a ɛtwa so a ɛde nnwuma ho a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, na ɛma adwuma a ɛyɛ denam nnyigye a ɛyɛ dɛnkyɛm a yɛbɛyɛ no mu ayɛ mmerɛw.
Nnwuma titirew a ɛyɛ mma yɛhunu ne yɛkyerɛ nnaano ne mfasoɔ a ɛyɛ mmoa no, ɛma yɛboa afiri nnaano ne mfasoɔ a ɛyɛ hwee a ɛyɛ mmoa a ɛyɛ mma yɛhunu ne yɛkyerɛ.
Ɛyɛ yɛn din no kwan ma ɛmo a yɛbɛfa abrabɔ bosɔn a ɛma yɛnhu mfaso ho nhoma, na ɛma yɛnhu yɛn adwuma a ɛwɔ yɛn nna mu.
Ɛwom sɛ AI wɔ hɔ sɛ nkyerɛkyire ahorow a ɛfa nsenkyerɛnne so, nanso AI yɛ komputa sayɛns no mu mmoa dwofo a ɛhwɛ nea ɛyɛ biako, nkyinhyia, na ɛwom sɛ yɛnnim nea ɛyɛ saa yɛbɛyɛ wɔ mmaa a ɛyɛ den mu.
Nnoboa a ɛyɛ sɛnkyerɛnni mu, na ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ yɛyɛ abɔdeɛ a ɛfa nneyɛ a wɔde yɛ abɔdeɛ a ɛhwehwɛ sɛ yɛhu bom.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea wɔboa, nkyekyɛmu ne nkyekyɛmu ahorow, sɛ woben kumanyɔn a ɛyɛ sɛ woben abofra a wohu afiri mu ne ahyehyɛde a ɛyɛ mfiase, nanso nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛyɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ, dwumase ne mmoa.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛnea nneɛma a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ abusuabɔ ahorow, a ɛwom sɛ wɔboa ama nnamda a ɛwɔ hɔ no.
AI din no, ɛyɛ mfi ase yɛ adwuma wɔ nhyehyɛso, aburokyere, abobɔdwam ne asomdwemerɛ mu, na ɛyɛ mfi ase abu so te sɛ nea ɛwɔ mmeae sɛnkyɛn ne video game nneɛma mu.
Ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ den koraa wɔ ɔkyekyɛ mu biara. Ɛne sɛ yɛte biara akyɛ sɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛni no bɛyɛ mfeɛsɛm a ɛnni bus no nteɛ.
Teknoloho ne din dadee a ɛma yɛbɛyɛ nhoma a yɛte kɔ so dwuma, ɛde biako a yɛbɛnya nkyɛn a ɛwɔ nkurase, yɛbɛnya nkran a ɛwɔ akwarium, aane yɛbɛnya mfonini a ɛyɛ sɛn a yɛwɔ hɔ no, nna yɛwɔ kwan so te sɛ yɛte nsraso a yɛyɛ no.
Nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔde nnwom kwan no yɛɛ adwuma no, ɛyɛ hu sɛ ɛyɛ paara biara nso sɛ woyi fi asu a ɛyɛ nnamfo no nkyɛn, na ɛma abɔdeɛ a ɛba fam no de asɛm a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a wɔde ma abɔdeɛ a ɛreba no.
Yɛbɛhyia sɛnea ɛte, afã horow a ɛyɛ mfe koro no, nnanom a ɛyɛ Bennet School manfo, ɛwɔ North Carolina, de website bi a ɛkyerɛ wɔn nkyɛn a ɛkɔ State Capital no ho. Mfe biara website no de bɛyɛ mfi, nanso nkyɛn a ɛyɛɛ hɔ bi ara yɛahu online sɛ ɛbɛyɛ abrabɔ a ɛkyerɛ nnwom.
Blogfoɔ no nso pɛ sɛ ɛboa abɔdwɛfoɔ abusuabɔ a ɛyɛ yɛ. Ɛwom sɛ abɔdwɛfoɔ biara tum bi akyi sɛ wɔbɔ mmaa no yɛ den na wonnya nkyɛn, sɛnea wɔwɔ ntampon a ɛyɛ papa no, ɛma ɛhwe ase.
Ɛfie a abɔdeɛfo no yɛ mmea ma denkyem, ɔkyerɛkyerɛni no hu sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ yiye no ato nkyɛnkyɛn a ɛbɛyɛ sɛ yɛmfa no bɔ ne ho mfub.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw akyi no nso na ɛma abɔdeɛ no ato nsa bo kyerɛ sɛ yɛte sɛe adwuma a ɛwɔ hɔ biara. Ɛyɛ awofoɔ no sɛnea wɔde abɔdeɛ no nansa a ɛma abɔdeɛ no nya nkɔso de, na ɛma wɔnyaa mmoa na nnya nkasa (Toto, 2004).
Bloggying no ne abɔde a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛbɛhyia biara, na ɛhyɛ kwan ma abɔfrafo ma adwuma kɔ so daben anaa asekyerɛ nnamyensa no nyinaa.
Nnwomtoa ahorow a yɛde yɛ yɛn ara nsa no, te sɛ blogs, betumi ama abɔfra akyerɛ sɛ wobɛyɛ mmoa na wobɛyɛ abrabɔfo; ɛfie kyerɛ sɛ, abɔfra no hyia mmaa a ɛwɔ internet so, na wobɛtumi abɔ no ho nkyere aseɛ wɔ akyire no mu nkyereɛ biara a akyirefo de di dwuma, na ɛkyɛn woma no ama no nkyereɛ n’adwuma ho nkyereɛ biara a ɛbɛyɛ no. (Oravec, 2002).
Ottawa yɛ Canada dinpa, ɛhɔ na ɛkyerɛ sɛ adwini foforo a ɛwɔ mmeae sɛnea ɛte no, na ɛwɔ nkwagye a ɛkyerɛ Canada nnyɛyɛ ahorow ne bre a ɛwɔ hɔ.
Niagara Fɔsɔ no ɛwɔ hɔ no kɔɔ fam, na nkyɛn no nso ɛyɛ muskoka ne nkyɛn a yɛanya biara mu no din.
Nyansa a ɛwɔ mmeaehwehwɛ yi nyina hɔ no, ne nwonwa biara a ɛyɛ sɛ ɛyɛ Kanada kɛseɛ no, abusuapanyin a ɛwɔ Ghana na ɛde ma wɔn a yɛanya wɔn hɔ.
Abɛn a ɛwɔ fam no, wɔn a ɛyɛ denam no nso, wɔn a wɔwɔ hɔ no yɛ fɛ, na ɛsono bi nso ɛyɛ asɛn so, ɛwom sɛ yɛnnya nipa pɛn.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea abɔde a ɛkyere sɛnea mmoa a ansa na ɛnyɛ yiye no: Amerikafo a ɛwɔ Amerika no, ɛyɛ sɛ mmoa a ɛwɔ Canada.
Nsramma a ɛwɔ Afrikaya Apueɛman no, ɛwɔ Nhyira Nhyira Man no mu, afrikanin atɔeɛ a ɛwɔ nkyɛn no ho.
Madagascar yɛ kɛseɛ no kɛseɛ, na ɛyɛ kontinent pɛn so no bio sɛnea ɛte sɛ faa akyi.
Mmoa pii a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ hɔ no yɛ man ahorow a ɛwɔ so, anaa ɛwɔ hyia ne France, na ɛyɛ din sɛ ɛyɛ mmerɛbea a ɛyɛ sɛnea wo afe ahyia.
Arabfo nso de Islam kɔɔ mmaa a, a ɛyɛɛ mfeɛ wɔ Komoros ne Mayotte man mu.
Ɛuropefoɔ dwadwene ne mmeahyɛn a ɛde maa mmeahyɛn fii ase efiri 15de afehyeɛ no, bere a Portuguesfoɔ abrafoɔ Vasco da Gama yii Cape Route no, ɛna ɛsii Europa fi India.
Afé hyia no, nsuhyia no ne Sahel ne ho bɛhyia, na anaafo ne nsansamfo no ne Atlantik Kɔsii no ne ho bɛhyia.
Ɛyɛ mpaapa sɛ obiara a ɔyɛ mmea na ɔreba no, ɔbɛka sɛ ɔyɛ ɔsofo, ɛwɔ mfeɛ no nso.
Ɛyɛ sɛ w’de nhwando a, afei na wo nso de gyɛ a, efisɛ nkyɛn a ɛyɛ dɔ no nko.
Ɛnna abofrafo no akyerɛ sɛ nnwuma a ɛyɛ den koraa no, ɛsɛ sɛ wohu sɛ mmeaeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛte sɛ ahwɛso a wobetumi de hyɛ no sɛ ɛyɛ ahayaso, na ɛnte sɛ ɛyɛ anaa. Ɛyɛ dabi a wobetumi de mpono kyɛ wo, wobetumi de nsa kyɛ wo, ne nea ɛkeka ho.
Mempɛ sɛ w’antumi nnye mmea a w’apere sɛ w’anhyira, na ɛnyɛ sɛ w’aha yiye sɛ woawofoɔ no (ɛwiem a ɛyɛ den kɛseɛ no, ɛnyɛ mmoa!).
Ɔbɔmaa Casablanca a ɛyɛ den no, Abibiremfo a na ɛdwaa hɔ a edi kan yɛɛ no wɔ afe 10 AD mfe nhyia a ɛyɛ mmiɛnsa hɔ, na Phoenicians, Ahomamisi, ne Merenids de dii sɛ adwuma a ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ beba no, wɔfrɛ no Anfa.
Ahafoɔ aboa no na ayɛn no foforo na w’akyiri Casa Branca, ɛna wosii no bio daakye sɛ earthquakes a ɛtɔ no so no, wɔde mmaa mu no.
Sultan no mu a ɛwɔ Morocco ne sɛnkyɛn no kɔɔ sii hɔn a ɛyɛ Daru l-Badya, a na ɛmaa no Casablanca din a ɛbɛnkyerefo a wɔde ntaa abotabata a ɛwɔ hɔ no bɛyɛɛ.
Casablanca ɛyɛ Morocco nyinaa mu asɛmpaka a ɛso sunsuma bi.
Berekyɛ Medina no atɔe no so, w’anya nnyigyei bebree a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔbɛtwa mogya a ɛyɛ mmoa, dɛnkyɛm, atwefire, pɔtɔpɔto, nanso ɛte sɛ yɛbɛyɛ ama aburokyerɛni.
Goma ne ahenkuro a ɛwɔ Democratic Republic of Congo, ɛwɔ apueɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ a ɛbɛyɛ Rwanda.
Abɔda 2002 mu no, Goma de dii nkyɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ yɛn ara, Nyiragongo wuom a ɛbɔɔ mmaa no yɛɛ, na ɛbɔɔ mpɔtam hɔ no agodie kɛse, wɔn a wɔte sɛ mpɔtam no nkwa.
Berekyerɛma Goma yɛ deɛn ara, nanso wobɛyɛ sɛ wobɛhwɛ sɛnea abotɔfɔ no te sɛn mu yɛ te kɔɔ fam North Kivu mantamu no nyinaa na ɛte sɛn.
Asebu no nso yɛ edin a wotumi bɛkyere Nyiragongo wutuo no, na ɛwɔ nso mponpon a ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛ wosiane Mountain Gorilla wɔ Afrika nyinaa mu.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wuhu bebree sɛ woanya boda-boda kɔ so Goma mu. Ɛno nkutoo no, ɛyɛ sɛ 500 Congolese Francs ma fekubere bi.
Nanso sɛnea ɛyɛ sɛ ɛma no ho mmerɛw a, "Timbuktu" ayɛ sɛnea yɛde ama apam a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, ɛkwan so te sɛ man no a ɛyɛ no ho mmerɛw.
Ɛda akyiri sɛ, Timbuktu ayɛ mfinfin nkyɛn no, nanso sɛnea ɛyɛ yiye koraa ma ɛyɛ abotakyiriɛ ahyɛn, na ɛwɔ asantewaa.
Ɔdaasɛn ahodo abɛduɔso ahasa ne aduɔnson a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu no, wɔyɛɛ no sɛ abɛduɔso a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ nnam, efisɛ asɔre asɔre bɛyɛ sɛnea ɛbɛfa.
Na ɛyɛ sɛ́nkyɛm a ɛyɛ denkyɛm a ɛkɔɔ so Henry Louis Gates PBS din a wɔfrɛ no Wonders of the African World no mu.
Ase nkyɛ a ɛyɛ denkyɛm koraa ne Ghana manfoɔ no nyinaa a ɛwɔ asɛnkuo biara mu, ɛfi na ɛwɔ mmeranteɛ a ɛyɛ Arabi koraa wɔ ha bi a, ɛnnyɛ Afrika biara.
Kruger National Park (KNP) no, South Africa atifi-atɔfoɔ fam no, ne Mozambique nhyease fam a ɛwɔ atifi, Zimbabwe nhyease fam a ɛwɔ atifi, na Crocodile River no ne kum no anim-anim.
Asase a ɛyɛ denkyem kwan 19,500 km² a ɛwɔ mfease, na ɛayɛ sɛnkyee ne duɔnko aduoson a ɛyɛ den, ɛde biara boa ahoka a ɛyɛ nwonwa.
Ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn pii wɔ South Africa a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn titiriisi a ɛwɔ South African National Parks (SANParks) mu.
Yɛte sɛ ɛte biara wɔ South Africa Manfoɔ Denam no mu, ɛwɔ dinnaa bi a wɔfa so yɛɛ abɔdeɛ ne sɛnea wobɛhyia mu yɛnna anaa.
Mepaakyɛ no, ɛyɛ sɛnea wo te sɛɛ sɛ wobɛboa Wild Card bi, a ɛma woanya afiri ahorow a ɛwɔ South Africa man mu, anaa South Africa nyɛnfa ahorow nyinaa.
Hong Kong Island no Hong Kong manfoɔ no din, na ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn a anompa a ansafoɔ pɛ sɛ ɛyɛ den koraa.
Hong Kong nkyim sɛn a ɛyɛ den no, ɛyɛ sɛ mmea a ɛdwo nanso ɛde hyɛw a, Victoria Harbour fi no ho akyiri no.
Hong Kong no nkyerew no nyinaa yɛ a, asɛmpaka no fi fam, na kɔ Kowloon apueɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ no so.
Hong Kong Island no nkabom nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛyɛ dɛn na ɛwɔ abopɔn no, wɔde bebree bi a ɛyɛ yɛyɛ a ɛwɔ atifi fam no so.
Ɛyɛ sɛdeɛ Britani amanpanin no ne wɔn de maa wɔn ho a, na yɛbɛhyia wo sɛ wosusu sɛ wobɛkyerɛ adwumayɛfoɔ abakɔsɛm no, ɛyɛ sɛnea wo de bɛfa no.
Sundarbans no ne apueɛ-mankwa a ɛyɛ denkyɛm sen biara ahyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ wiase, na ɛtɔ soɔ 80 kilomita (50 maili) kɔɔ Bangladeshi ne India manfoɔ abɔnten sɛnea ɛfi abofra hɔ.
Sundarbans no na ɛyɛ UNESCO Ɔmanfoɔ Nhyiamfoɔ Manfoɔ Boafoɔ Kyerɛwtoh. Sundarbans kwan so a ɛwɔ India so no, na ɛyɛ Sundarbans Manfoɔ Nhyiamfoɔ Park.
Ɛyɛ sɛ ɛsono no enti ara yɛ nkyene mangrove nkyekyem a ɛwɔ hɔ nko, nanso ɛwosɔ fam biara a ɛyɛ asɛm a ɛte sɛ abrafo a na ɛwɔ Gangetic daa ase no nyinaa.
Sundarbans no ntaa de kilomita skwer 3,850, na ɛsɛn a ɛyɛ mmienu a ɛyɛ pɔn no de mmeawa/abɔneɛ mu.
Abɛhyia 1966 bre a, Sundarbans no yɛɛ nkomase adwuma a ɛyɛ nkuraseɛfo dwadie, na ɛtɔ so asɛm sɛ ɛwɔ Bengal tigɛ a ɛyɛ hyɛw 400 ne abɔdeɛ pɔn a ɛyɛ mmerɛw 30,000 wɔ manfo no mu.
Ɔsono a ɛwɔ mmerante so no, ɛwɔ hɔ a yɛnya nkwan a ɛkyerɛ sɛ yebɛkɔ asɛmpapan no (apue a ɛwɔ apam so) na ɛwɔ hɔ daa biara, nanso bebree, ɛsɛ sɛ woyɛ bere a ɛne 06:30 ne 07:30 ara, ɛwom sɛ wosei kɔ agodɔ ne Jakar/Bumthang a ɛyɛ den.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw sɛ nnyansrafoɔ no boa a ɛwɔ hɔ no yɛ den, ɛyɛ sɛ wobɛboa bɛyɛ a ɛhɔ no din ama won a ɛyɛ akyiri.
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛbɛyɛ mfease no, nnwomto ahorɔw a ɛyɛ mfiase no na ɛwɔ hɔ, ɛwɔ mmɛnkuo bi a ɛyɛ mfiase a ɛwɔ Japan din "Coaster" a ɛyɛ nwanin, ɛyɛ mmerɛw ne ɛyɛ te sɛ twene.
Ɔkyekyɛ a yɛsom no yɛ mmaa a ɛyɛ mfiase a ɛma wo fi wo hɔ kɔ nkonya nansafo, te sɛ Paro (Nu 150) ne Punakha (Nu 200).
Ɔpona Oyapɔk a ɛyɛ kablɛ-stayed nti, ɛsra Oyapɔk Nsuo no, na ɛfa Oiapoque manfoɔ a ɛwɔ Brazil ne Saint-Georges de l'Oyapɔk manfoɔ a ɛwɔ French Guiana.
Mpamnoa no abien no trɔɔ abereɛ a ɛyɛ mita 83, ɛyɛ mita 378 afi, na ɛwɔ nkwataa abien a ɛyɛ mita 3.50 kwan.
Akokɔ a ɛwɔ abɔnten no mu no yɛ mita 15. Wobuee abɔnten no ahɔho wɔ Bososɛ 2011, nanso wonnyaa n'ahɔho de ama kwan soɔ no maa ɛbɛyɛ March 2017.
Apon no abusuafɔ no gyina sɛ ɛbɛyɛ sɛnea ɛbɛtena ase pɛpɛmpɛm wɔ Ɔbɛnem 2017 mu, bere a Brazilfo asɛn kwan no yɛbɛhyia ase.
Guaranífoɔ no, ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛnni ara a ɛwɔ hɔ bio a ɛyɛ mmea na ɛwɔ Apueɛ-Paraguay apueɛ fam, na ɛyɛ adwini a ɛte sɛ nnompeaso a nso na ɛyɛ nhyehyɛɛ fam bi.
Chaco mpɛsoa no, abofra ahenni ahorow biara wuraa hɔ, sɛdeɛ ɛyɛ sɛ Guaycurú ne Payaguá, a na ɛwɔ hɔ bi sɛ ɛkyerɛ sɛ na ɛwɔ ahonim, aboa ne nsua.
Ɔda a ɛmu yɛ 16 apam no, Paraguay, a na wɔfrɛ no "Nnipa Ho Asɔre Koro no Ani" akyiri sɛ, abusuakuw a wɔwoo no no, na ɛwoo nanso wɔn a wɔde di nso na ɛwɔ hɔ.
Ahafoɔ akyiri sɛnkyɛnno a ɛne sɛnkyɛnno mmienu no nyinaa kɔɔ so.
Abɛdwa ɛtoa Asunción a ɛtɔso no, Paraguay ayɛ di sɛ w’eduane ne nnamso deɛ ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ.
Argentina yɛ sɛn kɛseɛ sɛ wɔwɔ abbanedɛ bi a ɛyɛ den kɛseɛ ne abbanedɛfoɔ a ɛyɛ den kɛseɛ ahunuwɔm, afi mmaa no.
Ɔkyirew no de hyɛn no, ɔbɛyɛ December na ɛwɔ Las Cañitas polo kwan so no.
Nnwoma titiriw ne asɔre a ɛyɛ mfiase no nso, wɔde hu hɔ bebree wɔ afi ha biara mu.
Mekɔ kyɛ Asociacion Argentina de Polo sɛ w’afi yɛn ahyia fam no nna, na ɛyɛ sɛ wo bɛyɛ bi wo hyɛn polo nkyekyem a ne ho ahyia.
Ɛdeɛ biara a ɛyɛ sɛ, agyɛdin a wɔde fa fi Falkland a ɛne Falkland pound (FKP) sɛnkyɛre no, ne din dodo no yɛ sɛnkyɛre biako a ɛyɛ British pound (GBP) din.
Ɛden no mu no, ɛsono yɛboa w’akyekyɛ din saa a ɛwɔ Stanley, FIC West din a ɛwɔ hɔ no apuei.
Ɛsono a, sɛ́dɛɛ British pounds no nyinaa a ɛwɔ asase no nyinaa mu hwehwɛ sɛ ehyia, na Stanley ho nso credit cards a ɛyɛ Amerika dollar no nso mfeɛsɛm bɛyɛ a ɛte sɛɛ.
Ɛwom sɛnkyɛn a ɛwɔ manfoɔ no so, wobenya biara nni hɔ a wɔbɛhyia koodi kaat, ɛsɛ sɛ wode brittish a mmerica agyi din a wɔbɛhyia, yɛkyerɛ wo sɛ wobɛsra wodeɛ sɛ wodeɛ bɛyɛ payment a ɛte sɛnea.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw a wobɛyɛ sɛ wuhu Falklands dinara biara akyirikyiri nkyɛn a ɛwɔ asase no so, enti yɛhyɛ dinara kɔso akyiri sɛ woakɔ asase no anaa mu.
Ɛfie ne Montevideo a ɛwɔ Equator anim bɛyɛ fam, nna ɛyɛ mmerɛw wɔ ha no mu bre a, mprempɛn de ɛyɛ mmerɛw wɔ adwumam nhyeaso no mu na ɛyɛ mprempɛn wɔ ha no mu.
Montevideo no mu bi atɔeɛ abrabɔ a ɛyɛ den; ɛda akyiri no, afɔre nyinaa ɛyɛ +30°C dedaase.
Ɛyɛ sɛ winter no bɛyɛ sɛ ɛreteɛ, nanso ɛno nkra ehia koraa, na ɛsiane nhɔrekyereɛ ne nsuo, ɛma wo pɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mmerɛ bio sɛ thermometer no de akyerɛ no.
Ɛnnya mprempren "aberewa" ne "susuɔ" afɔre a; mmere a ɛdi so no, ɛde yɛ ama yɛnya mmɔfra de a ɛyɛ pɛpɛpɛpɛ.
Ɛwɔ sɛnea nansa pii a ɛwɔ manpanin no de wɔn ho hyɛ nkwaseɛ, nanso asasefa no ara bɛyɛ dɔnkyɛ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛmmfa nni dwetɛ a yɛmmfa yɛnya ntaban.
Ɛyɛ sɛ park no nnamfo akyerɛ sɛ, wobɛyɛ mfeɛsum adu akyi (100) na ɛsono ne akuraa biara akyi, na mfeɛsum num akyi (25) deɛ nso wobɛyɛ abofra foforo biara akyi!
Ɛyɛ sɛnea wobɛhyiaa no bio nso, bison, elk, moose, aberewa ne nnamfo dɔnhwerew a wɔn nyinaa yɛ den, ɛma wɔbɛyɛ mprempren.
Mfe biara, abrofo aha biara akyiri adwuma kakra wɔn ho akyi nti wɔtwaa nwonwa no ho asɛm. Ɛyɛ ntam, nwonwa biara yɛ den, ɛyɛ dɔ, enti ma wɔn nwonwa akyi.

Apia ɛyɛ Samoa kuw a ɛtɔ so. Ase no wɔ Upolu asase so, na ɛwɔ nipa dodoɔ a ɛyɛ mmienu ahanum aduokron, abubuo.
Apia noboa a ɛtɔso no 1850mmuo a ɛyɛ Samoa manfoɔ a ɛtwa so 1959 bre akyi.
Ɔdanso no na ɛyɛ edin no ntamgyina a ɛhɔ wɔ 1889 mu, bre a nnhwima a ɛsono mmienu no, Amerika, ne Britania, mmerɛ sɛ wɔbɛhyia Ɔdanso no.
Ɛyɛ sɛ ɛsono a wɔhyɛɛ no nyina hwee, efisɛ wobɔɔ mmea a ɛyɛ Britesikɔ no biara. Ɛsono num a ɛyɛ Amerikafo ne Agyemanfo no nyina hwee a, ɛyɛ biara nkyem pɛn nyina.
Berebi a Maufoɔ mmeaɛ no hyɛɛ abusuabɔ ahorow a ɛyɛ sɛ Ghana yɛhyɛn, abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ den kyerɛɛ asase no mu yii sɛ wɔtoo Tupua Tamasese Lealofi III, abusuapanyin no, no.
Auckland ɛwɔ apɔn ahorow kakra, nti ɛwɔ nsunoa a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu. Ɛsɛn no, ɛwɔ mmerɛ a ɛtɔ so num nanso a yɛde bɛhyia.
Nsraem a ɛwɔ North Harbour manfoɔ no, ɛwɔ Apam-no so, na ɛsɔrekyɛw wɔ Long Bay (atifi) kɔsi Devonport (atɔe).
Ɛsono a ɛyɛ sɛ mponua nyinaara a ɛwɔ mmea a ɛyɛ apɔn no, wɔn a wɔn nkyɛn a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, na ɛsono pii no ne pohutukawa nwuma a ɛma ɛyɛ hyew.
Tamaki Drive atɔeɛ a ɛwɔ Waitemata Harbour no, ɛwɔ Mission Bay ne St Heliers manfoɔ adanseɛ a ɛyɛ den wɔ Afehyiape Auckland man mu.
Ɛyɛ mmea ma no a ɛsono kɛseɛ sɛnkyɛnnee fam, na ɛwɔ mmea a ɛyɛ papa a ɛtwa fam no ho. Kookoo no yɛ de.
Aburo a ɛyɛ den no ne 'Number One', ɛnyɛ aburo a ɛte sɛɛ pii, nanso ɛyɛ sɛn na ɛma wo hyia. Ɛnnam aburo foforo a yɛfrɛ no 'Manta'.
Ɛwɔ pii a ɛyɛ Franço wines a ɛte sɛ de bɛtwa, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a, New Zealand na Australia wines no nso, wɔn a ɛnya yɛn ho a ɛyɛ mmerɛwa ma wɔn.
Mmera a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn no yɛ pɛ, na ɛnwom sɛ wo yɛ hwɛ kwan a, wo te sɛ wo pɛ mu no, wo hu botti-mmereɛ bio.
Afrikanfoɔ no ho, 'flat white' coffee no abotire biara nni hɔ. Mfena a ɛyɛ mmaa ne 'espresso', cappuccino no de nnam nketewa biara mu (mepɛ sɛ ɛno bɛyɛ frothy), na tee no yɛ deɛ ɛnyɛ susu biara ahyɛ.
Kakara a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛreɛ no yɛ bɛlgyiam anansesɛm. Apona a ɛyɛ mmera no yɛ yɛre pɛ sɛnea ɛte no, ɛno nso ɛyɛ yɛyɛ.
Ɛsono a ɛyɛ sɛnea wotumi abɔ wo ho no, wotumi kɔ reef no sɛnkyɛn, na ɛnyɛ mmerɛw sɛ woahu nhyira a ɛyɛ den sɛnea woboaboa reef no so.
Na ɛnyɛ, fa wohɔ ahorow sɛnea wɛnim de, yɛ nsiɛ akyire no nyinaa, na yɛ nteɛ ase pɛ sɛ wotutu wɔn atwene ahorow.
Abɔfra a w’adan no te sɛ aburo, wɔhwehwɛ wɔ mankyɛn mu no ne nsonsono fam a ɛwɔ fam 1770 a ɛwo hɔ, ɛbɛyɛ mmaa ɔbɛnem a ɛto abrɔpɔ ne apɛdedɛ. Sɛ wopɛ sɛ wohwehwɛ nnyɛ, ɛba nea ɛbɛyɛ.
Abofra a ɛwɔ hɔ, nanso ɛyɛ den sɛ wohuu nsadie. Ɛbɛɛ sɛ abofra no nyinaa hu nanso wonsu sɛ wɔnkɔ akɔ nkyɛn.
Abɔfo a ɛwɔ denkyemmua fam no nna wɔn adwuma nyinaa nanso wɔyɛ te sɛ nsuo a ɛwɔ apam fam no, w’ani nsi nea ɛwɔ nsupɔw no mu, na ɛte sɛ nsupɔw a ɛwɔ Rockhampton atifi no.
Abotire a ɛyɛ sɛ wode bɛyɛ no ara, na ɛma ɔyɛkyerɛma no anyɛ sɛ ɔbɛwo hɔ bi dehyɛ wo fie bere a ɔwɔ hɔ.
Abanfo a ɛyɛ nnyigyei no boa maa won a wuhu diɛ wɔ mmea a ɛwɔ hɔ a ɛyɛ pɛ, nanso ɛsɛ sɛ woanya firi abanfo no nso, ɛte sɛ manfo a ɛde nnaano so, sɛ woanya nnaano.
Agyawo a ɛyɛ mprempren no bɛyɛ sɛ woyi afiri a ɛde bɛhyia biara, nkyekyɛmu a ɛde kyɛ fa no kɔ/fi apuei, bɛyɛ sɛ abotan a ɛde abotam no ne nkunim a ɛde nkunim.
Ɛdeɛ biara, ɛma woahu sɛ wode nhoma no ayɛ wo sɛ wanya nkyerɛkyerɛ mu yɛnkyɛn a, anaa wɔn a ɛdeɛ biara a ɛyɛ wo ntummuase kɔ wo manfo’ no (efisɛ visa).
Wɔde biara yɛɛ nneɛma a na wɔpɛ sɛ yɛyɛ mfaase, na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde ma agyafo no ayɛ mfaase no di dwuma ɛna ɛnyɛ mfeaseɛ no, na ɛnyɛ hotel no animuonyamfo a wɔde bɛma no.
Ɔmanfoͻ a yɛde ayɛ afahyia biara mu no, ɔhaasifoͻ no nyinaa gu fi na wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a wͻn a w
Ɛna wobɛyɛ sɛ wode hyɛ ma den mu a, ɛsɛ woannya wo hɔ kɔe a ɛyɛ den ara ma woaso tentɛn kɔhwe akyi no.
Maada woa sɛnea ɛte sɛ, na ɛyɛ sɛ sika a ɛwɔ abɔnten so no ayɛhyia no, nanso ɛwom sɛ wutuntum a ɛwɔ asɔre no bɛyɛ adwuma kosii daakye.
Mfiase ahorɔw a wɔwɔ manfo' no, wɔwɔ mmerante' a ɛyɛ mmoa no nanso wɔn a wɔwɔ abɔnten a ɛyɛ den.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wode bɛyɛ Northern Baltic no wɔ abubu no mu a, yɛhyia kabin no din, ɛfie ne sɛ abubu no a ɛtaa ba a ɛma dwum a ɛyɛ pɛn sɛ wɔn a ɛtaa hyɛ nna no.
Saint Petersburg din no deɛ, ɛwɔ soro a ɛde ama wo kɔtaa man no mu. Cruise ahenni no nyinaa woma wɔn anni visa dehyɛ ne ho (hwɛ ne mponsem).
Mahaa a ɛyɛ mmoa a, wɔde nhyehyɛeɛ pii te sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ sɛnea abofra ahorow bɛyɛ denam mmoa ne nnwom. Windows ne nkata a wonnim no nso, ɛyɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔde yɛn nhyira ne ɛhono a ɛyɛ hwee a yɛnim no te sɛnea yɛbɛhwehwɛ hwɛ. **(A more natural-sounding and slightly more concise translation, prioritizing common usage):** Sika kɔkɔɔ mmea no bi a wɔyɛ, wɔde nhyehyɛeɛ pii te sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ sɛnea abofra a wɔbɛhwehwɛ ne nnwom no bɛyɛ den. Windows ne nkata no nso ɛyɛ sɛ wɔhwehwɛ a ɛnyɛ mfiase, na wusɛe no nyɛ yɛyɛ den.
Meda aseɛ, wobɛyɛ mmeɛa a wɔde mmoa, kakraa, ne nsɛm a ɛyɛ yɛyɛ, de yɛ ma wɔn yɛ mfonba a, na ɛde wɔn kɔ so hwɛ fam.
Akokɔɔ bi a ɛwɔ hɔ no de biribi a ɛyɛ denkyem a ɛma wɔnyaa bio pɛpɛɛpɛ. Nanso, nkwanta a ɛyɛ denkyem no taa ma wobɛhyiaa wo adwuma, na onipa a ɔkyere sɛ ɔyɛ ɔkyerɛkyerɛni biara yɛ te sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wubɛhyiaa wɔ biribiara mu.
Ɛte sɛnkyɛn a ɛnkɔ so wɔ aberew sɛ́deɛ a ɛyɛ den no, anaa wɔ asase ho a ɛyɛ prapra no, wɔn a wɔde kwan fi ase yɛbɛyɛ sɛ wohu sɛ ɛbɛtwa, hyɛn, anaa ɛbɛyɛ mmerɛw.
Ɛsɛ sɛ wode nnyigyei kwan so a ɛyɛ hyew na ɛwɔ firifiri so no, wobɛhwehwɛ sɛ wobɛkyerɛw sɛ wobɛte sɛ wode abɔde so a ɛwɔ hɔ mfa no.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛyɛ sɛ, nnawɔta bebree biara bi a ɛbɛyɛ sɛ woanyɛ no mu no, ɛsono a ɛyɛ nnyigyei biara te sɛɛ no de bɛma wo atwa atwa.
Mete so no, wobɛma woanwa akyiri no ama ɛyɛ hyia sen ara yɛbɛhyia bi, sɛnea ɛte sɛ snow a ɛna hã koraa a ɛyɛ mmɔfra no, anaa nsu a ɛyɛ dɔ a ɛwɔ so no, a ɛde sɛ nsuo a ɛyɛ hyew a ɛwɔ mpenani mu no.
Akodeɛ a, ɛyɛ sɛ mmea a ɛyɛ yɛyɛ a ɛwɔ mmea anaa ɛyɛ fipaa no de akyerɛ mmea pii, na wim sɛ wim te sɛ nea ɛyɛ berepɔn wɔ saa mmea no mu yɛ, na wim te sɛ nea ɛyɛ berepɔn wɔ saa mmea no mu yɛ.
Safari ahorow a ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛyɛ mmerɛw, na ɛyɛ abusuabɔ a anansesɛm kɛseɛ wɔ Afrika, na ɛyɛ abɛhyɛfoɔ pii no kwan no.
Mpra pɛ sɛ 'safari' ahodeɛ no, ɛyɛ sɛ wosow kwan abubu wɔ asase so, na woanya nwonkwa a ɛyɛ den wɔ Afrika, sɛnea ɛte biara nso wɔ savanna bi mu.
Mmeyɛ biara a, ɛwiem sɛ elefante ne giraffe a, wɔtaa yɛ adwuma kɛse sɛ wɔn a wɔbɛhyia car no afi, na mmea a ɛyɛ den no reba wo nkyɛn maa woho yɛ wo awoowɔ.
Mako, kyɛseɛ, na nkyɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ sɛ wone bɛyɛ akyire a ɛsɛ woahu wɔn yɛyɛ paa bio wɔ binocular mu.
Mfiridwuma a ɛyɛ sɛ wobɛhyia afã horow a ɛwɔ abɔso no (wɔfrɛ no "abɔso mfiridwuma", "ahyɛase mfiridwuma" anaa "wobɛtena afã") ne sɛ wobɛhyia afã, ama saa a ɛyɛ sɛ nnaawɔtwe biara ama daa biara.

Abotefuo bɛhwehwɛ nsewadee a ɛyɛ hwee sɛ wɔn manfoɔ no mu nso na ɛyɛ den.
Mensa no nte sɛ́ sɛ́ wosisi nnam, wɔn a ɛyɛ yɛn ho aharan, a na ɛyɛ huam a ɛyɛ nkonimdeɛ, wɔn a ɛsɔre mu, a na wɔtumi yɛ nokwarɛ, anaa wonsɔn nsonsono.
Mawu a ɛte sɛ mprempren, anaa nkyene a ɛboa ma nnaanoa a ɛbɛyɛ sɛ wɔbɔ wo din no, nnyɛ nsemmɔnea a yɛde bɛma obiara.
Abotaxin sen ?wɔ a ɛma woanya nnuan a wonnim taxes ne mpanyimfo adwuma bi wɔ beɛyɛ bi manfo? so.

Ɛna woakyere sɛ wo nni dwumako a ɛyɛ sɛ wo hyɛ nkontonkron akyi ara, yɛgye wo adwuma koraa: apam nketewa, nkyigyina te sɛ nkontonkron, ne nkwanta a ɛkeka a ɛwɔ hɔ pɛ.

Ahotefuo ahorow a ɛyɛ Germany manfo no nso wɔ amindɔn, hazelnuts, ne nkyene ahorow foforo. Mfiri a ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ a ɛso yɛ fɛwase koraa na ɛyɛ den koraa bio ama kakalika a ɛyɛ dwan.

Kari no yɛ nnam a ɛtaa yɛ herbs ne spices, te sɛ meat anaa ntrɛw a ɛyɛ ho.

Europa kontinent a ɛyɛ kɛseɛ no, nanso ɛwɔ manman adwuma ahorow a ɛyɛ pii. Ɛdeɛ sɛ wotumi a yɛyɛ mfiridwuma, ɛde biara nnyɛ visa na wo passport akyi no bɛyɛ pii.
Schengen bɛyɛ no, sɛnea ɛte biara, yɛde biako pɛ sɛ ɔman biara wɔ nneyɛe yi mu.
Ɛdeɛ sɛ wofi saa mpesa yi mu no, wɔawo a ɛyɛ a ɛma wukɔ so yɛ nkurow a ɛkyerɛ passport a ɛyɛ nnyigyi kwan no de.
Ɛyɛ sɛ, sɛ wode Schengen visa no a, ɛnyɛ kyɛ sɛ wode visa kɔɔ Schengen man ahorow no nyinaa kwan so, na ɛyɛ wo den kɔso, sika a ɛba fam, ne nkyekyɛm a ɛyɛ akyirikyiri.

Mmaa a wɔde nsaano ayɛ nna no, wɔte sɛ wɔyɛ nna nsoromma a ɛwɔ hɔ, nanso ɛyɛ fɛrekyereɛ sɛ nna a ɛyɛ massa no yɛ kɛse ara.
Agyapadeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ no yɛ paara a ɛyɛ denam sɛ́ Sámifoɔ no, na ɛna ɛsɛn koraa ma nnamfoɔ a wɔwɔ n’adwuma foforoɔ a ɛyɛ denam.
Akan biara, ɛnyɛ Sámi nyinaa na ɛwɔ hɔ a ɛyɛ adwuma biako pii wɔ abɔfoɔ nnan a ɛyɛ den, na ɛte sɛ nsuafoɔ, akuafoɔ ne nkyem, wo afe a ɛyɛ ntetee mu, wobɔɔ nkyɛn a wɔde hyɛn mfa wɔn te sɛ adwuma.
Ɛda akyiri sɛnea ɛte sɛ, adwuma a ɛyɛ denkyɛm a ɛwɔ mmea a ɛyɛ denkyɛm no mu, abɔde ahorow a ɛyɛ pɛ mu mmeɛnsa no boa afiri te sɛ nea ɛyɛ mmofra. Abɔde a ɛyɛ denkyɛm a ɛwɔ Sápmi, Sámifo no nanhyɛn a ɛyɛ denkyɛm no mu no, yɛ wo kyɛ sɛ nea ɛyɛ mmofra. **OR (a more natural/colloquial translation):** Daakye, Sámifo dɔɔsɔn a ɛyɛ denkyɛm no mu pii na ɛwɔ adwuma a ɛyɛ denkyɛm no mu. Ɛba saa ara, abɔde a ɛwɔ Sápmi, Sámifoɔ nanhyɛn no, yɛ denkyɛm.
Ɛwom sɛ ɛyɛ papa paa, ɛsɛ sɛ yɛmma yɛnnhwehwɛfo no, 'Gypsy' wɔfa no sɛ nkyereɛ a ɛyɛ huam no, nanso ɛbɛyɛ sɛ yɛnhwehwɛfo no ankasa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔde nnamso mmoawa na nkyereɛ ahorow a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, na ɛyɛ nnamso a ɛkyerɛ Romanifo.

Woye ne wo de sɛ wosusu so dwuma no, na wode sɛ woanyɛ nyɛnkyɛnii a ɛyɛ anaa wɔn manni a ɛyɛ wo manni no, nanso wɔn nkyekyɛm no ɛyɛ wɔn mmanpanin.
Yɛboa, sɛ nhwɛso bi a, Amerikafo a wɔwɔ Nsrammedua no mu no bɛhwehwɛ nea Akyiremanfo deɛ yɛ Arabfo no nso a ɛhwehwɛ so.
