Abrabo pii a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ mfasoɔ, na ɛma obiara atumi biara ayɛ mmerɛw a ɛbɛyɛ mfasoɔ, na ɛma nnipa nyinaa ayɛ mmerɛw a ɛbɛyɛ mfasoɔ, na ɛma nnipa anyɔnko no nya nkwa. **(Note: This is a complex sentence and a direct, elegant translation is challenging. This version aims for accuracy and comprehensibility. There might be slight variations depending on dialect. It essentially conveys the meaning of "severe weather" as encompassing dangerous phenomena that can cause damage, disruption, and loss of life.)**
Meteo a ɛyɛ yɛre, ɛba fa biara afi nhye, na ɛwɔ nnoaa ahorow a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, a ɛnte sɛ ɔman a ɛwɔ hɔ, abotakyiɛ na atmosfɛa no te sɛɛ.
Mmeɛ a ɛyɛ den, nnam, ɛsono a ɛteɛ, ne abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ nnam, ɛne atɔeɛ, akuraa a ɛfa, ne nnam-nnam a ɛyɛ kakrahwɛ.
Aberew a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ mmeranteɛ mu ne akyirikyiri a ɛwɔ nsonsonɔ mu no bi ne ɛkɔtɔ a ɛyɛ hyew, ɛkɔtɔ a ɛyɛ fitaa, ɛkɔtɔ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, ne abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ fitaa.
Mfaabɔfo no nyina sɛ wobɛyɛ denkyem biara a ɛbɛyɛ sɛ w’ani gye ho no, efisɛ ɛno no bɛma nea wode hyɛ ntaban a, yɛnnyɛ yɛn!
Ɔbenkyerɛ biara a ɛreyɛ sɛ ɔbɛfa bekyere a ɛte sɛ ntetee man no, ɛsɛ sɛ ɔnya nkyɛmu a ɛyɛ denkyem.
Akyigyina abrabɔ mu sɛ 'Hostile environment course' no bɛyɛ sɛ woahu sɛnea wobɛfa te sɛnkyɛn biara a ɛwɔ mane no so.
Kursu no biara a ɛyɛ sɛ wosusu ho no, afei na ɛbɛma woanya nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛyɛ den koraa a yɛakora so wɔ hɔ no, pɛpɛmpɛm nso na woanya abɔdeɛ a ɛtaa ba no.
Kwan no biara a ɛyɛ mfeɛ 2-5 na ɛbɛba fam, na ɛbɛhyia nkyigyisi, odwananan a ɛkyerɛ abobɔdwɛ, na ɛbɛyɛ biribiara nso abotireni sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ.
Abofra ne afoforo a ɛfa nkontompo mu nnaani ho no yɛ papa paa, sɛdeɛ ɛna abofra ne afoforo a ɛfa apampram a ɛtwe no yɛ kɛseɛ.
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo a ɛhyɛn sɛ wɔbɛyɛ mmea ahorow bi nanso wɔn a wɔde nnaano abɛyɛ nanso wɔn a wɔde nnaano abɛyɛ afi nhyeɛ a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔde nnwom nketewa a ɛde ama wɔn akwantu a ɛkɔ soro no. **Note:** This is a complex sentence, and a *perfectly* natural Twi translation would likely be much longer and more nuanced, potentially breaking it into multiple sentences for clarity. This translation attempts to maintain the original meaning within a single, albeit somewhat lengthy, Twi sentence. It utilizes phrasing common in discussing official travel and identification. Here's a breakdown of some key choices and why they were made: * **"Voyagers"**: "Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo" - this translates to 'travelers' or 'people travelling'. * **"Planning sex reassignment surgery"**: "ɛhyɛn sɛ wɔbɛyɛ mmea ahorow bi" - Literally: "they are thinking of doing certain womanly things". This is a circumlocution, as directly translating "sex reassignment surgery" is not common and would require lengthy explanation. A more literal approach could be *too* direct for some contexts. * **"Abroad"**: "afi nhyeɛ" – means 'from outside'. * **"Must ensure"**: "ɛyɛ sɛ" - meaning 'it is important that' or 'they should make sure'. * **"Valid documents"**: "nnwom nketewa" - meaning 'important papers/documents'. * **"Return trip"**: "akwantu a ɛkɔ soro no" – means 'the trip that goes up/back'.
Abusuapanyin afoforo de nnamsoɔ a wonya a wose anuanu wɔn nnamsoɔ mu (X) a na ma nnamsoɔ no nyε koraa wɔ nnamfoɔ a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔde di dwuma no na ɛyɛ den.
Abofra a ɛwɔ asɛmpapan a yɛn wo nanso a wɔn ahemfie no hyia biara nso nea ɛyɛ den no yɛ pɛ.
Ɛyɛ mfiase sɛnea wobɛhyia mu no, abofra a ɛyɛ den no ara akyi, wosusuw sɛ wosusuw wɔ mmea na ɛsɛn so.
Abofra a wonnya hwee kwan ma wonnkamfoɔ no, ɛnde wonnom yɛnnya nnamfoɔ ne nnsoroma a ɛyɛ den ma wɔn akyi.
Apono a ɛtwa so a ɛyɛ sɛnea mmere a ɛtso nkwa wɔ abɔnten so, de bedi nkyekyem a ɛwɔ manfo, sɛnea ɛte bi a ɛyɛ.
Ɛyɛ sɛ nsuo a ɛwɔ soro no ntamgyina hɔ a ɛyɛ den no nti, aponapon no boa saa mmea ɛyɛ den a ɛyɛ hɔ, na ɛmaa nsuo a ɛfa so te sɛ nkwantahwɛfɛ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛte so no bɛyɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ.
Ɔbarima a ɛyɛ senpɛn no na ɛwɔ hɔ sɛnea wobɛhyia mu no, ɛyɛ sɛ wobɛtena nnaano ase kɔso mpo a ɛte sɛ ɛbɛyɛ anaa.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wotɔ akyiri wo a, kɔɔ soro a ɛnnyɛ den kɛseɛ sɛ ɛte saa ara.
Yɛbɛhyia sɛ woanya daakye biara a wotumi anaa woanom yɛnkyɛ, aane de, sɛ wo nimdeɛ a wode ma wo, na ɛsɛ sɛ woakyekyere biara a wokum bi, yɛbɛkyerɛ wo sɛ woate sɛ woanom wo a, woanya nnyigye a woanya nsa a woanya yɛnkyɛ.
Akomma a wɔsan aba no, sɛ́né ébèyɛ denkyemkye biara, na ɛtaa ba no ntam no mmerɛw a ɛyɛ den, na ɛso te sɛ́ nea ɛyɛ den.
Abrokyirefo a ɛyɛɛ mmerɛw a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wosow kyɛ wɔn ntam no, sɛ wɔsan ba abotɔm kɔɔ n’asɔre a ɛyɛ mmerɛw no, ɛyɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ te sɛ mmerɛw kɛse.
Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ woakɔtena hɔ sɛ woanya ɔkyerɛkyerɛ wɔ mmea no mu a, woatumi anyɛ mmea a ɛyɛ den no afa so na woayɛ nhwɛsoɔ a ɛyɛ mfeɛ pii a ɛyɛ wo mmea no ntam. **(Alternative, slightly more concise version):** Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ woakɔtena hɔ akyiri sɛ woanya mmea foforo no nhyeɛ no, woatumi anyɛ wo mmea a ɛyɛ den no afa so na woayɛ nhwɛsoɔ a ɛyɛ mfeɛ pii a ɛyɛ wo mmea no ntam. **Explanation of choices and nuances:** * **Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ…:** "It will be that/as if..." - This sets up the conditional scenario. * **woakɔtena hɔ:** "You return home" - literally "you come back to the place." * **sɛ woanya ɔkyerɛkyerɛ wɔ mmea no mu:** "after living/receiving education/experience in a foreign land/culture" - "mmea" broadly means country, land, or culture. Using "ɔkyerɛkyerɛ" (education/experience) clarifies the "living abroad" aspect. "no mu" - "in it/them". * **woatumi anyɛ…afa so:** "you are able to let go of/discard…" – This expresses the idea of adapting and letting go of old habits. * **mmea a ɛyɛ den no:** “the strong/old culture” – referring to the original culture. * **woayɛ nhwɛsoɔ a ɛyɛ mfeɛ pii a ɛyɛ wo mmea no ntam:** “you have changed a lot from your culture” - literally "you have become a changed person a long time ago from your culture." "nhwɛsoɔ" means change/transformation. The slight variation provides a more streamlined phrasing, particularly removing redundancy. Both are valid translations, though.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wobɛyɛɛ mfeɛ a, abɔfo no ara maa wo ayɛ pa na wonsi wo anigye, wosusu sɛ onnimfo a ɛte sɛ wɔwɔ manpanin foforo mu no deɛ, wosua di nkɔso.
Abɛyɛ sɛ yɛnna anyɛ yɛbɛhyia sɛ abofra ne nhyira a ɛwɔ hɔ yɛmfa wɔn a ɛbɛsan kɔ nna no.
Pyramid no mu nsonson no kyerɛ sɛ, ɛyɛ mfeaseɛ no mu yɛɛ pa ara a ɛwɔ hɔ pɛ.
Wo te sɛ woanya nnhwɛso no mu nkyigyina, na wo te sɛ woanya nnhwɛso no mu mfa nea ɛyɛ hush hush a ɛbɛhyɛn no sɛe.

Sphinx no yɛ nkyɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ denkyɛm a na yɛbɛhwehwɛ, na ɔno nso yɛ mmeɛnsa a ɛka adeɛ biara a ɛyɛ mmerɛw.

Sodifo no a ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ kilomita 120 atifi fam wɔ Peninsulakuro no so. Ɛyɛ kɛseɛ King George Island na ɛwɔ Villa Las Estrellas manfoɔ.
Ɛbibiman mu nso wɔ Livingston Island ne Deception, a ɛwɔ apue koraa a ɛyɛ mmeranteɛ a volcano bi a ɛte sɛe sɛ w’atumi de bɛyɛ denkyem a ɛyɛ denkyem no.
Ellsworth Manfoɔ no Peninsulani atifi fam no, na Bellingshausen Denkyem a ɛwɔ fam no ne ne nsono.
Asase a ɛwɔ Peninsulani hɔ no, wɔn nkyɛnkyɛn nyinaa kakraa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ nkyɛn a ɛyɛ den no, na ɛsɔ hwɛ ma ɛyɛ platɔ, afei nanso ɛsɔ aba maa ɛyɛ Ellsworth Mountains a ɛyɛ kilomita 360 a ɛwɔ soro, a Minnesota Glacier de nea ɛyɛ pɛn pɛn di dwuma bɛyɛ awo.
Antarctica atifi a ɛyɛ den no, ne nyinaa mu no, ɛwɔ mfiridwuma a ɛde sɛ Sentinel Range, a Vinson Massif no, ɛtɔ so 4892 m Mount Vinson.
Ɛwɔ mmeaɛsoɔ ahorow no, sɛ cell phone nni hwee a, satellite phone de bɛyɛ wo deɛ wo nte sɛe no.
Satelefon a ɛyɛ mpanin no nni saa ara na ɛbɛyɛ mobile telefon no abasu, efisɛ wo te sɛ wobɛyɛ mmaa a wonnya nkyɛn sɛ wobɛboa afiri a ɛwɔ apuei no ara na woabɛyɛ wobɛboa afiri.
Wɔde adehyɛ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛwɔ hɔ no yɛ denkyem, akyiri yi mmoa a ɛyɛ mfasoɔ, nso wɔde ama abrabɔfo a wosusu sɛ wɔyɛ data ne nwom pɛpɛpɛpɛ a ɛyɛ denkyem.
W’ababoadee a wɔde ama wo manfoɔ no de bɛboa wo mfa mu yɛ sɛnea wobɛyɛ sɛ woanya afi horow mu.
Mmoa a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ den koraa ma wɔn a ɛsɛn sɛ wɔhyia gap-year no, ne sɛ wɔte so kɔ so yɛ adwuma na wɔn nso mmɔ wɔn ho.
Ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ sɛnea abɔde ahorow a ɛdi so te sɛn no, na ɛma wɔnya afɔso biara a edi hɔ ma adwuma a ɛntua adwuma a ɛdi hɔ ma nnwompa a wɔde bɛhyia afi asɛm no. **A more natural and concise translation would be:** Na ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ wɔ abɔde ahorow a ɛdi so te sɛn no mu, na ɛma wɔanya afɔso biara a edi hɔ ma adwuma a ɛntua adwuma a ɛdi hɔ ma nnwompa a wɔde bɛhyia afi asɛm no. **Even more concise and commonly used:** Ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ wɔ abɔde a ɛdi so te sɛn no mu, na ɛma wɔnya afɔso biara a edi hɔ ma adwuma a ɛntua adwuma a wɔde bɛhyia afi asɛm no.
Ɛte sɛnkyɛn mu no, ɛyɛ a wobɛyɛ gap-year nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ nkyɛn a ɛnyɛ wo man mu, na ɛboa wo sɛ wobɛnya mfeɛ panyin nkyɛn mu nkyɛn a ɛwɔ wo kurom a ɛyɛ wo.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wosua adwuma krono koraa na woanya abodin mu nsramma yi.
Finland yɛ nkurow a ɛyɛ pɛ sɛ w’abɔden. ‘Nkurow biako man’ no nso wɔ nkurow pii no mu, a ɛwɔ nkurow mu no na ɛwɔ apɔn no mu a ɛyɛ mmerɛwa.
Maha a ɛwɔ apueɛ ne nsunoa mu no, ɛnyɛ deɛ wobɛhwe yacht bio.
Ɛwom sɛ adwini dwumase ne nkontonkoro titire ahorɔw no yɛ nwonwa koraa ma yɛakyɛ biara, nanso nsaase a ɛyɛ mmerɛw bio a ɛyɛ sɛ nkwataa biara a na anaa even kayak no boa ma ɛhyehyeɛ foforo.

Ɛsono kɛseɛ bi a wɔde hyɛ nkyerɛkyerɛ mu no, Berlin, Germany na ɛwɔ hɔ. Sɛ wode map no abue, wo te sɛ Berlin ɛnyɛ denkyemnaa hɔ nanso ɛsono no nhyehyɛɛeɛ no nni kum no mu.

Ɛsono dwuma ne nyansa a ɛwɔ hɔ ma yɛnhwɛ sɛnea nnyigyi a ɛyɛ adwuma te sɛnea yɛyɛ, na ɛma yɛahu sɛnea ɛte so wɔ nhwehwɛ a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛyɛ no mu no, akyiri yi a ɛma obiara a w’ani gu so a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛyɛ a ɛbɛyɛ den. Ɛna abofrafoɔ a ɛkyerɛ nneɛma yɛ deɛ ɛyɛ denkyem koraa sɛ wɔde nneɛma akyɛ na wotumi de nneɛma a wɔde hyɛ no ma no nkutoo. Bere nyinaa, abrabɔ ne nneɛma a ɛkyerɛ nneɛma, nneɛma a ɛyɛ denkyem, ne nneɛma a ɛyɛ sɛ wode bɛkyɛ no ma ɛyɛ nnwuma a ɛyɛ denkyem.
Ɛte sɛnkyɛn pii de, abɔdeɛ a ɛyɛ den no ne nyansa a wɔwɔ wɔn so, nanso ama nkyekyem a ɛyɛ mmerɛw, ne abɔdeɛ a ɛnyɛ den no ne mmere bi a ɛyɛ dɔɔso.
Ɛna wɔde yɛn akyɛn sɛ wɔde nneɛma kɔ so dwuma, ɛte sɛ nneɛma a wɔde frafra no, wɔn a wɔyɛ mmeaeɛ no de nnaa biara pɛn na ɛyɛ adwuma anaa ɛyɛ ahomahyeɛ.

Moldova no kuromanan no Chişinău ɛyɛ. Ɛhafoɔ kwan no Romanian yɛ, nanso Russian de bɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Moldova yɛ manman a ɛwɔ mmofra a ɛyɛ mmerante sɛnkyɛn a ɛtaa hyɛ bɔne ma nneɛma a ɛyɛ den.
Abɔdaa a ɛne 1994 mu no, na ɛtaafo no hyɛɛ Moldova apuee fam no mu Transnistria Republic a wɔde hyɛɛ ase, a ɛwɔ nkunim ahorow ne sika koropɔn a ɛyɛ sɛ w’anyaa mfaso afiri biara UN mmarima mmea no mu.
Ate sɛnkyɛm ahorow a ɛwɔ Moldova mmaa ketewa no ntam, abotɔw a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛm a ɛyɛ mmeae biara nni hɔ da so, na ɛbɛyɛ sɛ wɔde nea ɛyɛ adwuma ne adwinsa a ɛyɛ mmeae biara nni hɔ no so hyɛn.
Moldova man mu yɛɛ ɛsɛm no kɛseɛ ne Ɔsofo Kristoni.
İzmir, Tɔɔfa no mu nkyɛn a ɛtɔ so nnan no, ɛwɔ nifubuɔ bi a ɛyɛ makoɔ pɛnnam deɛ, ɛyɛ Istanbul akyiɛ no abofra bi a ɛyɛ den, na ɛyɛ kwan so te sɛɛ a ɛyɛ yɛ.
Bere bi ɛyɛ Smyrna adwini ahorow, ɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛ denkyem, abusuafotuo, ne nimdeɛ a ɛyɛ baa fam, a ɛwɔ kookoo bi mu, na nkyirifi a ɛyɛ mmeranteɛ no de yɛn bɛn.
Ɛsɛn no, nkontonkron kete, glass-panom abrabɔ ne mmea a ɛyɛ mmoa no, wim wɔn a wɔwɔ abɔdeɛ nnwɛso a ɛyɛ fitaa hɔ, aparɔkuma a ɛwɔ asaase mmiɛnsa, ne mmeɛ a ɛyɛ gɔɔden ne nkwantanan, nanso obubɔ a ɛwɔ mfinfini no yɛ sɛ ɛyɛ Europa man a ɛwɔ mmere a ɛyɛ denkyem, ɛnyɛ Turkey so nko.
Haldarsvík manfo no ne Eysturoy apam no ho mfa ho, na wɔ w’abɔde foforo a ɛyɛ mmea nnan.
Ɔkyirew nsramma mu no, wosow dɔm a ɛyɛ mmerɛw deɛ ɛwɔ marbɔl a ɛwɔ dwumahini biara so.
Ɛyɛ mfeɛ pɛn a ɛde sɛ wohoho wɔ mmea a ɛyɛ den no mu.
Afeeɛ sɛ́pére na ɛyɛ mféase, Sintra manpanin no, ɛyɛ adwuma kakra pɛ, na Lord Byron ne mfasoɔ a ɔkyɛree no ayɛ no ama abrofoɔ no ho nimdeɛ.
Scotturb deɛdɛ 403 yɛ Sintra kɔso, na ɛyɛ Cabo da Roca nkyɛn.
Nanso afa atifi no, fa wo kɔ Fatima Nyankopɔn Maame Dwadie (Abɔso Dwadie) a yɛte sɛ Yesu Kristo nyankopɔn a ɛyɛ den koraa a ɛyɛ din no ho.
Medaase sɛ wuhu sɛ wo reteɛ yɛ bɛyɛ dɛnkyira a ɛyɛ mmeranteɛ no, na ɛyɛ man no mu apamfoɔ biara nso, sɛnea ɛte sɛ, nnipa dodɔɔ ara a atwa ho a wɔ wuraeɛ wɔ wiase nyinaa mu no.
Ɛwɔ mmea na mmɛnnum pii a ɛhɔ kɔsii sɛ wɔdii wɔn ho wɔ hɔ, na mmea foforo nso a wɔn nwoa a wɔkoaa a wɔhɔ na anaa wɔde hyɛɛ asaase so, Abrofɛ ne Abrofɛ mmaa a yɛn nyinaa.
Mepɛ sɛ woaanya saa kwan no nyansa, nhyira na woahyira no. Ɛnyɛ mmoa sɛ wode ahayɛ Holocaust a na Nazi dwenee no.
Medaase, nnyɛ nsaanoa kyɛn fa biara a ɛyɛ sɛ wo bɛte graffito so, a na wo de kɔ so, anaa wo bɛyɛ nsua wɔ nnanfa biara mu.
Barcelona no kyerɛ Catalan a ɛne Spanish sɛ yɛdeɛ biara. Ɛsono a ɛyɛ hɔ no, wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔhwehwɛ Catalan no yɛ pɛpɛpɛpɛ, nnipa pii no nso wɔn a wɔte Catalan ase no yɛ pii, na wobɛyɛ biara pɛ Spanish.
Nanso, wobɛyɛ sɛnea ɛte sɛdeɛ, wobɔde nkyerɛkyerɛ ahorow no Catalan kasa mu nkoara, ɛfie ne nimdee sɛ ɛyɛ mmea a ɛtwa so asɛmpka no.
Nanso, Spanish nso yɛ wie koroa wɔ abɔdeɛ ne afoforo ho.
Ɛyɛ sɛ Metro no mu yɛ regular nnanananoa no Catalan kasa mu no, nanso nneɛma a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛpo no, automated system de kɔmaa wɔn kasa biara mu, a ɛwɔ Spanish, English, French, Arabic, ne Japanese.
Parisians biara w’adwuma bi, w’ani nnya n’efiri sɛ w’ani yɛ sɛe, w’ani gyina hɔ na w’ani yɛ baa.
Ɛwom sɛ ɛyɛ mpaninfo a ɛnyɛ yiye no, ɛde biara nte sɛ wofiri Paris mu no, wo deɛ woyɛ wo mfaahyen ho sɛ wotumi yɛ nneyɛe a ɛyɛ dɛ. Ɛbɛma wo nnya wo nwini wɔ hɔ a ɛyɛ mmerɛw.
Paarisi foɔ no abusuabɔ ahorɔw biara a wotumi hu no no akyiri no, ɛno nso akyiri sɛ wode abusuabɔ a ɛyɛ dɛ ahomegye ma no no.
Plitvice Lakes bosum a ɛyɛ densus, nnipa dwoodi biara nni hɔ, esɛm sɛ beech, spruce, ne fir nkyene a ɛwɔ hɔ, na ɛwɔ Alpine ne Mediterranean nturuso a ɛyɛ pɛ sɛ nso.
Ɛwɔ mmea bosom a ɛyɛ den koraa, efisɛ wobɛhyia nneyeeɛ a ɛyɛ den, asase a ɛyɛ foforo na ɛhɔ no nso, na apuei a ɛyɛ foforo.
Mmerɛ no nso ɛyɛ dɔmfoɔ a ɛwɔ nnamfoɔ ne nnubɔfoɔ ahorow pii.
Ɛsono a ɛyɛ denkyɛm sɛnea ɛbɛbrɛfo brukumɔ, apem, nkwantankora, nwɛso, abɔkyewaa, adɔkuru ne kokorɔkɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ no, ne nsonosɛm a ɛte sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ no, wɔhwehwɛ sɛ woakyi.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ adwuma bi a, abofrafo deɛ wɔreba abosom fapɔn no, wɔntua mma wɔn akyiri a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn nnaa yɛ dɔn, na wɔn apow no nso ɛsɛ sɛ ɛte so.
Ɛsono a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔde nkyɛn a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a wɔde maa abofra a w’ani gyi so no, nanso ɛgerɛ wo a wobɛfa wo nkyɛn koraa, ɛsɛ sɛ ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn a ɛwɔ mmerɛ so te sɛ sɛ wo yɛ ma wo a ɛyɛ mfiase no.
Ɛyɛ mmesua a, mmɛnnum na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn yɛ nkwantanan a ɛsra afɔre.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wone no nso ara yɛte sɛ wode bɛhyia afi enɔm nnaano, nanso abɔde no ɛnnya ahwashɛ da so da so ara yɛanya koraa a wode yɛn ama wo nnyɛ, na ɛno nti mmaa no, wubehu sɛ wobɛyɛ nnyɛ. Mema yɛn nyinaa! (For men!) **OR (a more natural sounding alternative, depending on context):** Woara no nso ara yɛte sɛ wode bɛhyia afi enɔm nnaano, sɛtey abɔde no ɛnnya ahwashɛ dema yɛn nyinaa a yɛde yɛn ama; ɛno nti ɛsɛ sɛ wubehu sɛ wobɛyɛ nnyɛ. Ɛyɛ mma yɛn nyinaa! (For men!) **Explanation of choices & nuances:** * **"This too can be borrowed..."**: "Ɛyɛ sɛ wone no nso ara yɛte sɛ wode bɛhyia afi..." (It is that this too, we understand that you can borrow from...). "Woara no nso" also works ("You can also take this…"). * **"...stock at the entrance"**: "enɔm nnaano" – literally "entrance place". * **"...isn't washed after every user"**: "abɔde no ɛnnya ahwashɛ da so da so ara" - "the clothing doesn't get washed after use, after use." A more concise, natural-sounding way is “abɔde no ɛnnya ahwashɛ dema yɛn nyinaa” – “the clothing isn’t washed for all of us”. * **"...you may not feel comfortable wearing these skirts"**: "wubehu sɛ wobɛyɛ nnyɛ" – "you should be careful/expect that you won’t be comfortable.” or "wɛanya koraa a wode yɛn ama wo nnyɛ" - "you won't be too comfortable with what we give you." * **"One size fits all for men!"**: "Mema yɛn nyinaa!" or “Ɛyɛ mma yɛn nyinaa!” – literally "It fits all of us!" The "for men!" is implicit but could be clarified with "mma yɛn nyinaa!" used after the statement, as shown in the translation. The best translation depends on the specific context and the level of formality desired. I've provided two options to give you a choice.

Mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den no nkyɛnkyɛn a ɛwɔ hɔ biara a ɛyɛ mmerɛw wɔ saaɛ bere yi, na ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ abusuabɔ ahorow, anaa nkyɛnkyɛn nhyeaseɛ.
Ɛfie a na ɛyɛ den no, na ɛnnyɛ yɛn nhyehyɛe dwo a ɛwɔ hɔ nhyia bi a ɛyɛ den kyɛn, na ɛwɔ mmanpanin kete a ɛyɛ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den ara. Na ɛyɛ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den a ɛyɛ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den kyɛn a wɔayɛ no. **(A more natural and slightly simplified version, prioritizing flow and common usage, is below. The first version is a very literal translation.)** Na ɛyɛ den no, sɛ na ɛnnyɛ yɛn nhyehyɛe dwo a ɛwɔ hɔ nhyia bi a ɛyɛ den kyɛn, yɛahu no nanso na ɛyɛ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den kyɛn a wɔayɛ no. Na ɛyɛ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den kyɛn a ɛyɛ mfeɛ a ɛyɛ den kyɛn a wɔayɛ no.
Ɛsono a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛnso wɔ mfeɛ no nyinaa a wɔde yɛ nhomaapanin nhyehyɛe no, wɛnɛ ne nnwuma a ɛwɔ nkwakwanfoɔ so a ɛyɛ den wɔ abapɔn fam a ɛyɛ yɛn ara man.
Ɔkyerɛw a ɛyɛ sɛ cherry blossom a ɛyɛ denkyem, a wɔfrɛ no hanami, no wɔ Japanfo kasa mu no, ɛyɛ nnamsoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ bi wɔ Japanfo adwinni mu no, efii afe apaeduo (8th century) kosii sɛnea ɛte bi.
Abɔdeɛ no fii China, ɛwɔ hɔ nso, adɔm biara bɛyɛe plum blossoms no na ɛyɛɛ beae a wɔpɛ.
Japan man mu no, abɔdeɛ a ɛto so dwan ahoforo no, na wɔde hyɛɛ adwumawɔn a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛn mu no, na empena kyɛɛ ne ho na nso kyɛɛ manpanin a ɛwɔ manpanin apɛdeɛ mu no.
Mmea no bebree bio wɔ ntaban kwan so, enti yɛhyia mfaso sɛ woanya biako pɛ akyi.
Ɛna sɛ wosɔ hwɛ garden a ɛyɛ sɛnea yɛde bɛma no, wobɛhyia wo pɛn, ɛwom sɛ wode akataso koraa.
Singapore yɛ man a ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ nanso ɛyɛ mmerɛw, na wobɛyɛ sɛ wobɛyɛ nhwehwɛma kɛseɛ no, na woho bɛtumi ayɛ nneɛma biara wɔ hɔ nkyɛn a wo redi so.
Nanso sɛ woyɛ "apam nipa ho" a ɛwɔ equator atifi fam no, ɛsɛ sɛ wo hu amam (seesei) na nsunkum sɛe a ɛyɛ mmerɛw (efisɛ asase so no nnya ase, ɛnte sɛ mmerɛw).
Ɛwɔ nso nkurow a ɛkɔ nɔfuo fam Hebron, w’adze a Yeboa Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, ne mmofraa a wɔdɔ no nyinaa yɛbɛyɛ ntam.
Hwɛ sɛ ɔkwan a wo yɛbɛhyia no nya Hebron, ɛnyɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ Kiryat Arba a ɛwɔ hɔ no.
Asaase mpoano deɛ ɛyɛ sɛnea wotumi de nhoma a ɛkyerɛ sɛnea woafere ho ahyia no.
Mɛkyɛ sɛ, wobɛyɛ mfiridwuma de nkurow a ɛwɔ Loire Valley no mu, Rhine Valley no mu, anaa woanya nsafoforo kɔ mmea a ɛyɛ ho nwonwa a ɛwɔ Danube no so, anaa woanya nwa no ato Erie Canal so.
Na ɛyɛ mmea ma aponopɔn ho sɛnea wɔbɛfa nna nwoma a ɛyɛ den kakra no.
Krismas yɛ Kristoni abɔde ahorow a ɛyɛ den koraa bi, na ɛhyiam wo sɛ Yesu wo wo no din.
Ɛsono a ɛwɔ hɔ no, abɔdeɛ a wonnya Kristoni a ɛwɔ Kristoni manmua ne abɔdeɛ a wonnya Kristoni a ɛwɔ wiase nyinaa de nea ɛyɛ sɛnea wɔyɛ no bɛyɛ.

Wɔ mmeaeɛ a, ɛwɔ Kristoni nyansahu ahorow a ɛkyerɛ saa asɛm yi, nanso ɛte sɛ nea ɛyɛ Kristoni asan ayɛ akyiri a, na ɛyɛ abɔdeɛ ne mmea ahorow a ɛyɛ sɛnkyɛnni.
Abakɔsɛm a ɛyɛ dwin a ɛyɛ sɛ, nnamfoɔ ahyehyɛdeɛ no bi a ɛyɛ sɛ wƆde Easter Vigil a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔde ahɔhɔdwo fie bi a ɛwɔ Easter abakɔsɛm no mu, na ɛhyehyɛdeɛ no biara a ɛbɛyɛ dɔnko a ɛbɛyɛ mmaa mmienu a ɛwɔ daa hwehwɛ a ɛwɔ Kristo asɛmpase no so.
Nyansafua biara a ɛbɛyɛɛ sɛnea wɔbɛyɛɛ kwan so, a ɛbɛyɛɛ fam so, anaa ɛbɛyɛɛ mpoano so na ɛbɛyɛɛ asase no.
Afé a nkontaa a ɛyɛ denam no, nkyenkyɛn a wɔn a wɔte sɛ wobɛfa so no nni hɔ, na ɛmaa asantewaa a ɛyɛ dwo a ɛyɛ nwonwa no no nkyɛnkyɛn a ɛyɛ pɛn no wɔ Galapagos.
Abrɛpɔn a ɛdi soɔ no, ɛwɔ Galapagos biara so, ahyɛyɛɛ mmoa pii sɛ goat, kuda, asɛm, nketewa, abusua a ɛyɛ abɔdeɛ ne adanko.
Ɛna wobɛyɛ Arctic anaa Antarctic manna mu nyinaa abɛdua no, wobɛhu polar daa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔdehyɛfa biara nni hɔ a wonnyaa yɛnkyim.
Ɛyɛ sɛnea wo de bɛyɛ sɛ wobɛkyerɛ aurora borealis no ho, efisɛ anaa yɛbɛhyia anaa yɛnte saa te sɛ sɛ obiara bɛtumi de hyɛn.
Ébɛyɛ sɛ nnwomto no ara yɛ bɛyɛ pii, na ɛna ɛyɛ sɛ nnam yɛ yɛn ho ahyia, enti wo de bɛhunu nyansrafoɔ.
Asase pa a ɛwɔ Japan no yɛ mmerɛw a ɛyɛ denkyɛm na ɛyɛ abotakora, ɛno nso wɔn a wɔwo hɔ no anum yɛnso no nni dwuma koraa.
Ɛyɛ sɛ wim sɛn no ne mmoa a ɛyɛ sɛ woadwuma, na nnamfo de mfeannipa nnɔm a, yɛn de abɔdeɛ no a wɔde yɛ wo dwumfoɔ ne nnɔm a ɛyɛ sɛ woadwuma.
Abotare a ɛyɛ mmerɛw a ɛso, ɛnyɛ mpa a yɛde ma nnipa panyin no, na ɛyɛ mpa a yɛde ma abotare nyinaa.
Agyawfo bebua biara sɛ wɛnkyi a wɔde ma no na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ agyawfo no nkyere biara a wɔde ma no nyina, na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ agyawfo no ama biara a wɔka no wɔn a wɔyɛ agyawfo no akyɛ.
